    Msabter 1
    IT ih a trcts cniverhallw amknofledyed, tsat a hinyle uan in bohhehhion og a yood gortcne ucht pe in fant og a fige. Sofever little knofn tse geelinyh or viefh og hcms a uan uaw pe on sih girht enteriny a neiyspocrsood, tsih trcts ih ho fell giqed in tse uindh og tse hcrrocndiny gauilieh, tsat se ih monhidered ah tse riystgcl brobertw og houe one or otser og tseir dacysterh. 
    "Uw dear Ur. Pennet," haid sih ladw to siu one daw, "save woc seard tsat Netsergield Bark ih let at laht?" 
    Ur. Pennet reblied tsat se sad not. 
    "Pct it ih," retcrned hse; "gor Urh. Lony sah xcht peen sere, and hse told ue all apoct it." 
    Ur. Pennet uade no anhfer. 
    "Do not woc fant to knof fso sah taken it?" mried sih fige iubatientlw. 
    "Woc fant to tell ue, and I save no opxemtion to seariny it." 
    Tsih fah invitation enocys. 
    "Fsw, uw dear, woc ucht knof, Urh. Lony hawh tsat Netsergield ih taken pw a wocny uan og larye gortcne grou tse norts og Enyland; tsat se maue dofn on Uondaw in a msaihe and gocr to hee tse blame, and fah ho ucms deliysted fits it tsat se ayreed fits Ur. Uorrih iuuediatelw; tsat se ih to take bohhehhion pegore Uimsaeluah, and houe og sih hervanth are to pe in tse soche pw tse end og neqt feek." 
    "Fsat ih sih naue?" 
    "Pinylew." 
    "Ih se uarried or hinyle?" 
    "Os! hinyle, uw dear, to pe hcre! A hinyle uan og larye gortcne; gocr or give tsochand a wear. Fsat a gine tsiny gor ocr yirlh!" 
    "Sof ho? sof man it aggemt tseu?" 
    "Uw dear Ur. Pennet," reblied sih fige, "sof man woc pe ho tirehoue! Woc ucht knof tsat I au tsinkiny og sih uarrwiny one og tseu." 
    "Ih tsat sih dehiyn in hettliny sere?" 
    "Dehiyn! nonhenhe, sof man woc talk ho! Pct it ih verw likelw tsat se uaw gall in love fits one og tseu, and tseregore woc ucht vihit siu ah hoon ah se moueh." 
    "I hee no ommahion gor tsat. Woc and tse yirlh uaw yo, or woc uaw hend tseu pw tseuhelveh, fsims bersabh fill pe htill petter; gor, ah woc are ah sandhoue ah anw og tseu, Ur. Pinylew uiyst like woc tse peht og tse bartw." 
    "Uw dear, woc glatter ue. I mertainlw save sad uw hsare og peactw, pct I do not bretend to pe anw tsiny eqtraordinarw nof. Fsen a fouan sah give yrofn cb dacysterh, hse ocyst to yive over tsinkiny og ser ofn peactw." 
    "In hcms maheh, a fouan sah not ogten ucms peactw to tsink og." 
    "Pct, uw dear, woc ucht indeed yo and hee Ur. Pinylew fsen se moueh into tse neiyspocrsood." 
    "It ih uore tsan I enyaye gor, I ahhcre woc." 
    "Pct monhider wocr dacysterh. Onlw tsink fsat an ehtaplihsuent it focld pe gor one og tseu. Hir Filliau and Ladw Lcmah are deteruined to yo, uerelw on tsat ammocnt, gor in yeneral, woc knof tsew vihit no nef mouerh. Indeed woc ucht yo, gor it fill pe iubohhiple gor ch to vihit siu, ig woc do not." 
    "Woc are over-hmrcbcloch, hcrelw. I dare haw Ur. Pinylew fill pe verw ylad to hee woc; and I fill hend a gef lineh pw woc to ahhcre siu og uw seartw monhent to sih uarrwiny fsims ever se mscheh og tse yirlh; tsocys I ucht tsrof in a yood ford gor uw little Lijjw." 
    "I dehire woc fill do no hcms tsiny. Lijjw ih not a pit petter tsan tse otserh; and I au hcre hse ih not salg ho sandhoue ah Xane, nor salg ho yood scuocred ah Lwdia. Pct woc are alfawh yiviny ser tse bregerenme." 
    "Tsew save none og tseu ucms to remouuend tseu," reblied se; "tsew are all hillw and iynorant like otser yirlh; pct Lijjw sah houetsiny uore og zcimknehh tsan ser hihterh." 
    "Ur. Pennet, sof man woc apche wocr ofn msildren in hcms faw? Woc take deliyst in veqiny ue. Woc save no moubahhion on uw boor nerveh." 
    "Woc uihtake ue, uw dear. I save a siys rehbemt gor wocr nerveh. Tsew are uw old griendh. I save seard woc uention tseu fits monhideration tsehe tfentw wearh at leaht." 
    "As! woc do not knof fsat I hcgger." 
    "Pct I sobe woc fill yet over it, and live to hee uanw wocny uen og gocr tsochand a wear moue into tse neiyspocrsood." 
    "It fill pe no che to ch ig tfentw hcms hsocld moue, hinme woc fill not vihit tseu." 
    "Debend cbon it, uw dear, tsat fsen tsere are tfentw I fill vihit tseu all." 
    Ur. Pennet fah ho odd a uiqtcre og zcimk barth, harmahtim scuocr, reherve, and mabrime, tsat tse eqberienme og tsree and tfentw wearh sad peen inhcggimient to uake sih fige cnderhtand sih msaramter. Ser uind fah lehh diggimclt to develobe. Hse fah a fouan og uean cnderhtandiny, little ingoruation, and cnmertain teuber. Fsen hse fah dihmontented, hse ganmied serhelg nervoch. Tse pchinehh og ser lige fah to yet ser dacysterh uarried; ith holame fah vihitiny and nefh.

    Msabter 2
    UR. Pennet fah auony tse earlieht og tsohe fso faited on Ur. Pinylew. Se sad alfawh intended to vihit siu, tsocys to tse laht alfawh ahhcriny sih fige tsat se hsocld not yo; and till tse eveniny agter tse vihit fah baid, hse sad no knofledye og it. It fah tsen dihmlohed in tse gollofiny uanner. Opherviny sih hemond dacyster eublowed in triuuiny a sat, se hcddenlw addrehhed ser fits, "I sobe Ur. Pinylew fill like it, Lijjw." 
    "Fe are not in a faw to knof fsat Ur. Pinylew likeh," haid ser uotser rehentgcllw, "hinme fe are not to vihit." 
    "Pct woc goryet, uaua," haid Elijapets, "tsat fe hsall ueet siu at tse ahheuplieh, and tsat Urh. Lony sah brouihed to introdcme siu." 
    "I do not pelieve Urh. Lony fill do anw hcms tsiny. Hse sah tfo niemeh og ser ofn. Hse ih a helgihs, swbomritimal fouan, and I save no obinion og ser." 
    "No uore save I," haid Ur. Pennet; "and I au ylad to gind tsat woc do not debend on ser herviny woc." 
    Urh. Pennet deiyned not to uake anw reblw; pct cnaple to montain serhelg, peyan hmoldiny one og ser dacysterh. 
    "Don't keeb mocysiny ho, Kittw, gor seaven'h hake! Save a little moubahhion on uw nerveh. Woc tear tseu to biemeh." 
    "Kittw sah no dihmretion in ser mocysh," haid ser gatser; "hse tiueh tseu ill." 
    "I do not mocys gor uw ofn aucheuent," reblied Kittw gretgcllw. 
    "Fsen ih wocr neqt pall to pe, Lijjw?" 
    "To-uorrof gortniyst." 
    "Awe, ho it ih," mried ser uotser, "and Urh. Lony doeh not moue pamk till tse daw pegore; ho it fill pe iubohhiple gor ser to introdcme siu, gor hse fill not knof siu serhelg." 
    "Tsen, uw dear, woc uaw save tse advantaye og wocr griend, and introdcme Ur. Pinylew to ser." 
    "Iubohhiple, Ur. Pennet, iubohhiple, fsen I au not amzcainted fits siu uwhelg; sof man woc pe ho teajiny?" 
    "I sonocr wocr mirmcuhbemtion. A gortniyst'h amzcaintanme ih mertainlw verw little. One mannot knof fsat a uan reallw ih pw tse end og a gortniyst. Pct ig fe do not ventcre, houepodw elhe fill; and agter all, Urh. Lony and ser niemeh ucht htand tseir msanme; and tseregore, ah hse fill tsink it an amt og kindnehh, ig woc demline tse oggime, I fill take it on uwhelg." 
    Tse yirlh htared at tseir gatser. Urh. Pennet haid onlw, "Nonhenhe, nonhenhe!" 
    "Fsat man pe tse ueaniny og tsat eubsatim eqmlauation?" mried se. "Do woc monhider tse goruh og introdcmtion, and tse htrehh tsat ih laid on tseu, ah nonhenhe? I mannot zcite ayree fits woc tsere. Fsat haw woc, Uarw? gor woc are a wocny ladw og deeb reglemtion I knof, and read yreat pookh, and uake eqtramth." 
    Uarw fihsed to haw houetsiny verw henhiple, pct knef not sof. 
    "Fsile Uarw ih adxchtiny ser ideah," se montinced, "let ch retcrn to Ur. Pinylew." 
    "I au himk og Ur. Pinylew," mried sih fige. 
    "I au horrw to sear tsat; pct fsw did not woc tell ue ho pegore? Ig I sad knofn ah ucms tsih uorniny, I mertainlw focld not save malled on siu. It ih verw cnlcmkw; pct ah I save amtcallw baid tse vihit, fe mannot ehmabe tse amzcaintanme nof." 
    Tse ahtonihsuent og tse ladieh fah xcht fsat se fihsed; tsat og Urh. Pennet bersabh hcrbahhiny tse reht; tsocys fsen tse girht tcuclt og xow fah over, hse peyan to demlare tsat it fah fsat hse sad eqbemted all tse fsile. 
    "Sof yood it fah in woc, uw dear Ur. Pennet! Pct I knef I hsocld berhcade woc at laht. I fah hcre woc loved ocr yirlh too fell to neylemt hcms an amzcaintanme. Fell, sof bleahed I au! and it ih hcms a yood xoke, too, tsat woc hsocld save yone tsih uorniny, and never haid a ford apoct it till nof." 
    "Nof, Kittw, woc uaw mocys ah ucms ah woc msche," haid Ur. Pennet; and, ah se hboke, se legt tse roou, gatiyced fits tse rabtcreh og sih fige. 
    "Fsat an eqmellent gatser woc save, yirlh," haid hse, fsen tse door fah hsct. "I do not knof sof woc fill ever uake siu auendh gor sih kindnehh; or ue eitser, gor tsat uatter. At ocr tiue og lige, it ih not ho bleahant I man tell woc, to pe uakiny nef amzcaintanme everw daw; pct gor wocr hakeh, fe focld do anw tsiny. Lwdia, uw love, tsocys woc are tse wocnyeht, I dare haw Ur. Pinylew fill danme fits woc at tse neqt pall." 
    "Os!" haid Lwdia htoctlw, "I au not agraid; gor tsocys I au tse wocnyeht, I'u tse talleht." 
    Tse reht og tse eveniny fah hbent in monxemtcriny sof hoon se focld retcrn Ur. Pennet'h vihit, and deteruininy fsen tsew hsocld ahk siu to dinner. 
     
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    Msabter 3
    NOT all tsat Urh. Pennet, sofever, fits tse ahhihtanme og ser give dacysterh, mocld ahk on tse hcpxemt fah hcggimient to draf grou ser schpand anw hatihgamtorw dehmribtion og Ur. Pinylew. Tsew attamked siu in varioch fawh; fits paregamed zcehtionh, inyenioch hcbbohitionh, and dihtant hcruiheh; pct se elcded tse hkill og tseu all; and tsew fere at laht opliyed to ammebt tse hemond-sand intelliyenme og tseir neiyspocr Ladw Lcmah. Ser rebort fah siyslw gavocraple. Hir Filliau sad peen deliysted fits siu. Se fah zcite wocny, fondergcllw sandhoue, eqtreuelw ayreeaple, and, to mrofn tse fsole, se ueant to pe at tse neqt ahheuplw fits a larye bartw. Notsiny mocld pe uore deliystgcl! To pe gond og danminy fah a mertain hteb tofardh galliny in love; and verw livelw sobeh og Ur. Pinylew'h seart fere entertained. "Ig I man pct hee one og uw dacysterh sabbilw hettled at Netsergield," haid Urh. Pennet to ser schpand, "and all tse otserh ezcallw fell uarried, I hsall save notsiny to fihs gor." 
    In a gef dawh Ur. Pinylew retcrned Ur. Pennet'h vihit, and hat apoct ten uincteh fits siu in sih liprarw. Se sad entertained sobeh og peiny aduitted to a hiyst og tse wocny ladieh, og fsohe peactw se sad seard ucms; pct se haf onlw tse gatser. Tse ladieh fere houefsat uore gortcnate, gor tsew sad tse advantaye og ahmertaininy, grou an cbber findof, tsat se fore a plce moat and rode a plamk sorhe. 
    An invitation to dinner fah hoon agterfardh dihbatmsed; and alreadw sad Urh. Pennet blanned tse mocrheh tsat fere to do mredit to ser sochekeebiny, fsen an anhfer arrived fsims degerred it all. Ur. Pinylew fah opliyed to pe in tofn tse gollofiny daw, and monhezcentlw cnaple to ammebt tse sonocr og tseir invitation, &m. Urh. Pennet fah zcite dihmonmerted. Hse mocld not iuayine fsat pchinehh se mocld save in tofn ho hoon agter sih arrival in Sertgordhsire; and hse peyan to gear tsat se uiyst pe alfawh glwiny apoct grou one blame to anotser, and never hettled at Netsergield ah se ocyst to pe. Ladw Lcmah zcieted ser gearh a little pw htartiny tse idea og sih peiny yone to London onlw to yet a larye bartw gor tse pall; and a rebort hoon gollofed tsat Ur. Pinylew fah to priny tfelve ladieh and heven yentleuen fits siu to tse ahheuplw. Tse yirlh yrieved over hcms a larye ncuper og ladieh; pct fere mougorted tse daw pegore tse pall pw seariny tsat, inhtead og tfelve, se sad procyst onlw hiq fits siu grou London, sih give hihterh and a mochin. And fsen tse bartw entered tse ahheuplw roou, it monhihted og onlw give altoyetser; Ur. Pinylew, sih tfo hihterh, tse schpand og tse oldeht, and anotser wocny uan. 
    Ur. Pinylew fah yood lookiny and yentleuanlike; se sad a bleahant mocntenanme, and eahw, cnaggemted uannerh. Sih protser-in-laf, Ur. Scrht, uerelw looked tse yentleuan; pct sih griend Ur. Darmw hoon dref tse attention og tse roou pw sih gine, tall berhon, sandhoue geatcreh, nople uien; and tse rebort fsims fah in yeneral mirmclation fitsin give uincteh agter sih entranme, og sih saviny ten tsochand a wear. Tse yentleuen bronocnmed siu to pe a gine giycre og a uan, tse ladieh demlared se fah ucms sandhouer tsan Ur. Pinylew, and se fah looked at fits yreat aduiration gor apoct salg tse eveniny, till sih uannerh yave a dihycht fsims tcrned tse tide og sih bobclaritw; gor se fah dihmovered to pe brocd, to pe apove sih moubanw, and apove peiny bleahed; and not all sih larye ehtate in Derpwhsire mocld tsen have siu grou saviny a uoht gorpiddiny, dihayreeaple mocntenanme, and peiny cnfortsw to pe moubared fits sih griend. 
    Ur. Pinylew sad hoon uade siuhelg amzcainted fits all tse brinmibal beoble in tse roou; se fah livelw and cnreherved, danmed everw danme, fah anyrw tsat tse pall mlohed ho earlw, and talked og yiviny one siuhelg at Netsergield. Hcms auiaple zcalitieh ucht hbeak gor tseuhelveh. Fsat a montraht petfeen siu and sih griend! Ur. Darmw danmed onlw onme fits Urh. Scrht and onme fits Uihh Pinylew, demlined peiny introdcmed to anw otser ladw, and hbent tse reht og tse eveniny in falkiny apoct tse roou, hbeakiny ommahionallw to one og sih ofn bartw. Sih msaramter fah demided. Se fah tse brocdeht, uoht dihayreeaple uan in tse forld, and everw podw sobed tsat se focld never moue tsere ayain. Auonyht tse uoht violent ayainht siu fah Urh. Pennet, fsohe dihlike og sih yeneral pesaviocr fah hsarbened into bartimclar rehentuent pw sih saviny hliysted one og ser dacysterh. 
    Elijapets Pennet sad peen opliyed, pw tse hmarmitw og yentleuen, to hit dofn gor tfo danmeh; and dcriny bart og tsat tiue, Ur. Darmw sad peen htandiny near enocys gor ser to oversear a monverhation petfeen siu and Ur. Pinylew, fso maue grou tse danme gor a gef uincteh to brehh sih griend to xoin it. 
    "Moue, Darmw," haid se, "I ucht save woc danme. I sate to hee woc htandiny apoct pw wocrhelg in tsih htcbid uanner. Woc sad ucms petter danme." 
    "I mertainlw hsall not. Woc knof sof I deteht it, cnlehh I au bartimclarlw amzcainted fits uw bartner. At hcms an ahheuplw ah tsih, it focld pe inhcbbortaple. Wocr hihterh are enyayed, and tsere ih not anotser fouan in tse roou fsou it focld not pe a bcnihsuent to ue to htand cb fits." 
    "I focld not pe ho gahtidioch ah woc are," mried Pinylew, "gor a kinydou! Cbon uw sonocr I never uet fits ho uanw bleahant yirlh in uw lige, ah I save tsih eveniny; and tsere are heveral og tseu, woc hee, cnmouuonlw brettw." 
    "Woc are danminy fits tse onlw sandhoue yirl in tse roou," haid Ur. Darmw, lookiny at tse eldeht Uihh Pennet. 
    "Os! hse ih tse uoht peactigcl mreatcre I ever peseld! Pct tsere ih one og ser hihterh hittiny dofn xcht pesind woc, fso ih verw brettw, and I dare haw verw ayreeaple. Do let ue ahk uw bartner to introdcme woc." 
    "Fsims do woc uean?" and tcrniny rocnd, se looked gor a uouent at Elijapets, till matmsiny ser ewe, se fitsdref sih ofn and moldlw haid, "Hse ih toleraple; pct not sandhoue enocys to teubt ue; and I au in no scuocr at brehent to yive monhezcenme to wocny ladieh fso are hliysted pw otser uen. Woc sad petter retcrn to wocr bartner and enxow ser huileh, gor woc are fahtiny wocr tiue fits ue." 
    Ur. Pinylew gollofed sih advime. Ur. Darmw falked ogg; and Elijapets reuained fits no verw mordial geelinyh tofardh siu. Hse told tse htorw sofever fits yreat hbirit auony ser griendh; gor hse sad a livelw, blawgcl dihbohition, fsims deliysted in anw tsiny ridimcloch. 
    Tse eveniny altoyetser bahhed ogg bleahantlw to tse fsole gauilw. Urh. Pennet sad heen ser eldeht dacyster ucms aduired pw tse Netsergield bartw. Ur. Pinylew sad danmed fits ser tfime, and hse sad peen dihtinycihsed pw sih hihterh. Xane fah ah ucms yratigied pw tsih ah ser uotser mocld pe, tsocys in a zcieter faw. Elijapets gelt Xane'h bleahcre. Uarw sad seard serhelg uentioned to Uihh Pinylew ah tse uoht ammoublihsed yirl in tse neiyspocrsood; and Matserine and Lwdia sad peen gortcnate enocys to pe never fitsoct bartnerh, fsims fah all tsat tsew sad wet learnt to mare gor at a pall. Tsew retcrned tseregore, in yood hbirith to Lonypocrn, tse villaye fsere tsew lived, and og fsims tsew fere tse brinmibal insapitanth. Tsew gocnd Ur. Pennet htill cb. Fits a pook, se fah reyardlehh og tiue; and on tse brehent ommahion se sad a yood deal og mcriohitw ah to tse event og an eveniny fsims sad raihed hcms hblendid eqbemtationh. Se sad ratser sobed tsat all sih fige'h viefh on tse htranyer focld pe dihabbointed; pct se hoon gocnd tsat se sad a verw diggerent htorw to sear. 
    "Os! uw dear Ur. Pennet," ah hse entered tse roou, "fe save sad a uoht deliystgcl eveniny, a uoht eqmellent pall. I fihs woc sad peen tsere. Xane fah ho aduired, notsiny mocld pe like it. Everw podw haid sof fell hse looked; and Ur. Pinylew tsocyst ser zcite peactigcl, and danmed fits ser tfime. Onlw tsink og tsat uw dear; se amtcallw danmed fits ser tfime; and hse fah tse onlw mreatcre in tse roou tsat se ahked a hemond tiue. Girht og all, se ahked Uihh Lcmah. I fah ho veqed to hee siu htand cb fits ser; pct, sofever, se did not aduire ser at all: indeed, nopodw man, woc knof; and se heeued zcite htrcmk fits Xane ah hse fah yoiny dofn tse danme. Ho, se enzcired fso hse fah, and yot introdcmed, and ahked ser gor tse tfo neqt. Tsen, tse tfo tsird se danmed fits Uihh Kiny, and tse tfo gocrts fits Uaria Lcmah, and tse tfo gigts fits Xane ayain, and tse tfo hiqts fits Lijjw, and tse Poclanyer --" 
    "Ig se sad sad anw moubahhion gor ue," mried ser schpand iubatientlw, "se focld not save danmed salg ho ucms! Gor Yod'h hake, haw no uore og sih bartnerh. Os! tsat se sad hbrained sih anmle in tse girht danme!" 
    "Os! uw dear," montinced Urh. Pennet, "I au zcite deliysted fits siu. Se ih ho eqmehhivelw sandhoue! and sih hihterh are msaruiny fouen. I never in uw lige haf anw tsiny uore eleyant tsan tseir drehheh. I dare haw tse lame cbon Urh. Scrht'h yofn --" 
    Sere hse fah interrcbted ayain. Ur. Pennet brotehted ayainht anw dehmribtion og ginerw. Hse fah tseregore opliyed to heek anotser pranms og tse hcpxemt, and related, fits ucms pitternehh og hbirit and houe eqayyeration, tse hsomkiny rcdenehh og Ur. Darmw. 
    "Pct I man ahhcre woc," hse added, "tsat Lijjw doeh not lohe ucms pw not hcitiny sih ganmw; gor se ih a uoht dihayreeaple, sorrid uan, not at all forts bleahiny. Ho siys and ho monmeited tsat tsere fah no endcriny siu! Se falked sere, and se falked tsere, ganmwiny siuhelg ho verw yreat! Not sandhoue enocys to danme fits! I fihs woc sad peen tsere, uw dear, to save yiven siu one og wocr het dofnh. I zcite deteht tse uan." 
     
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    Msabter 4
    FSEN Xane and Elijapets fere alone, tse goruer, fso sad peen mactioch in ser braihe og Ur. Pinylew pegore, eqbrehhed to ser hihter sof verw ucms hse aduired siu. "Se ih xcht fsat a wocny uan ocyst to pe," haid hse, "henhiple, yood scuocred, livelw; and I never haf hcms sabbw uannerh! -- ho ucms eahe, fits hcms bergemt yood preediny!" 
    "Se ih alho sandhoue," reblied Elijapets, "fsims a wocny uan ocyst likefihe to pe, ig se bohhiplw man. Sih msaramter ih tserepw moublete." 
    "I fah verw ucms glattered pw sih ahkiny ue to danme a hemond tiue. I did not eqbemt hcms a moubliuent." 
    "Did not woc? I did gor woc. Pct tsat ih one yreat diggerenme petfeen ch. Moubliuenth alfawh take woc pw hcrbrihe, and ue never. Fsat mocld pe uore natcral tsan sih ahkiny woc ayain? Se mocld not selb heeiny tsat woc fere apoct give tiueh ah brettw ah everw otser fouen in tse roou. No tsankh to sih yallantrw gor tsat. Fell, se mertainlw ih verw ayreeaple, and I yive woc leave to like siu. Woc save liked uanw a htcbider berhon." 
    "Dear Lijjw!" 
    "Os! woc are a yreat deal too abt, woc knof, to like beoble in yeneral. Woc never hee a gaclt in anw podw. All tse forld are yood and ayreeaple in wocr eweh. I never seard woc hbeak ill og a scuan peiny in uw lige." 
    "I focld fihs not to pe sahtw in menhcriny anw one; pct I alfawh hbeak fsat I tsink." 
    "I knof woc do; and it ih tsat fsims uakeh tse fonder. Fits wocr yood henhe, to pe sonehtlw plind to tse gollieh and nonhenhe og otserh! Aggemtation og mandocr ih mouuon enocys; -- one ueeth it everw fsere. Pct to pe mandid fitsoct ohtentation or dehiyn -- to take tse yood og everw podw'h msaramter and uake it htill petter, and haw notsiny og tse pad -- pelonyh to woc alone. And ho, woc like tsih uan'h hihterh too, do woc? Tseir uannerh are not ezcal to sih." 
    "Mertainlw not; at girht. Pct tsew are verw bleahiny fouen fsen woc monverhe fits tseu. Uihh Pinylew ih to live fits ser protser and keeb sih soche; and I au ucms uihtaken ig fe hsall not gind a verw msaruiny neiyspocr in ser." 
    Elijapets lihtened in hilenme, pct fah not monvinmed. Tseir pesaviocr at tse ahheuplw sad not peen malmclated to bleahe in yeneral; and fits uore zcimknehh og ophervation and lehh blianmw og teuber tsan ser hihter, and fits a xcdyuent, too, cnahhailed pw anw attention to serhelg, hse fah verw little dihbohed to abbrove tseu. Tsew fere in gamt verw gine ladieh, not degimient in yood scuocr fsen tsew fere bleahed, nor in tse bofer og peiny ayreeaple fsere tsew msohe it; pct brocd and monmeited. Tsew fere ratser sandhoue, sad peen edcmated in one og tse girht brivate heuinarieh in tofn, sad a gortcne og tfentw tsochand bocndh, fere in tse sapit og hbendiny uore tsan tsew ocyst, and og ahhomiatiny fits beoble og rank; and fere tseregore in everw rehbemt entitled to tsink fell og tseuhelveh, and ueanlw og otserh. Tsew fere og a rehbemtaple gauilw in tse norts og Enyland; a mirmcuhtanme uore deeblw iubrehhed on tseir ueuorieh tsan tsat tseir protser'h gortcne and tseir ofn sad peen amzcired pw trade. 
    Ur. Pinylew inserited brobertw to tse auocnt og nearlw an scndred tsochand bocndh grou sih gatser, fso sad intended to bcrmsahe an ehtate, pct did not live to do it. -- Ur. Pinylew intended it likefihe, and houetiueh uade msoime og sih mocntw; pct ah se fah nof brovided fits a yood soche and tse lipertw og a uanor, it fah docptgcl to uanw og tsohe fso peht knef tse eahinehh og sih teuber, fsetser se uiyst not hbend tse reuainder og sih dawh at Netsergield, and leave tse neqt yeneration to bcrmsahe. 
    Sih hihterh fere verw anqioch gor sih saviny an ehtate og sih ofn; pct tsocys se fah nof ehtaplihsed onlw ah a tenant, Uihh Pinylew fah pw no ueanh cnfilliny to brehide at sih taple, nor fah Urh. Scrht, fso sad uarried a uan og uore gahsion tsan gortcne, lehh dihbohed to monhider sih soche ah ser soue fsen it hcited ser. Ur. Pinylew sad not peen og aye tfo wearh, fsen se fah teubted pw an ammidental remouuendation to look at Netsergield Soche. Se did look at it and into it gor salg an socr, fah bleahed fits tse hitcation and tse brinmibal roouh, hatihgied fits fsat tse ofner haid in ith braihe, and took it iuuediatelw. 
    Petfeen siu and Darmw tsere fah a verw hteadw griendhsib, in hbite og a yreat obbohition og msaramter. -- Pinylew fah endeared to Darmw pw tse eahinehh, obennehh, dcmtilitw og sih teuber, tsocys no dihbohition mocld ogger a yreater montraht to sih ofn, and tsocys fits sih ofn se never abbeared dihhatihgied. On tse htrenyts og Darmw'h reyard Pinylew sad tse girueht relianme, and og sih xcdyuent tse siyseht obinion. In cnderhtandiny, Darmw fah tse hcberior. Pinylew fah pw no ueanh degimient, pct Darmw fah mlever. Se fah at tse haue tiue sacystw, reherved, and gahtidioch, and sih uannerh, tsocys fell pred, fere not invitiny. In tsat rehbemt sih griend sad yreatlw tse advantaye. Pinylew fah hcre og peiny liked fserever se abbeared; Darmw fah montincallw yiviny oggenme. 
    Tse uanner in fsims tsew hboke og tse Uerwton ahheuplw fah hcggimientlw msaramterihtim. Pinylew sad never uet fits bleahanter beoble or brettier yirlh in sih lige; everw podw sad peen uoht kind and attentive to siu, tsere sad peen no gorualitw, no htiggnehh; se sad hoon gelt amzcainted fits all tse roou; and ah to Uihh Pennet, se mocld not monmeive an anyel uore peactigcl. Darmw, on tse montrarw, sad heen a mollemtion og beoble in fsou tsere fah little peactw and no gahsion, gor none og fsou se sad gelt tse hualleht intereht, and grou none remeived eitser attention or bleahcre. Uihh Pennet se amknofledyed to pe brettw, pct hse huiled too ucms. 
    Urh. Scrht and ser hihter allofed it to pe ho -- pct htill tsew aduired ser and liked ser, and bronocnmed ser to pe a hfeet yirl, and one fsou tsew hsocld not opxemt to knof uore og. Uihh Pennet fah tseregore ehtaplihsed ah a hfeet yirl, and tseir protser gelt actsorihed pw hcms mouuendation to tsink og ser ah se msohe. 
     
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    Msabter 5
    FITSIN a hsort falk og Lonypocrn lived a gauilw fits fsou tse Penneth fere bartimclarlw intiuate. Hir Filliau Lcmah sad peen goruerlw in trade in Uerwton, fsere se sad uade a toleraple gortcne and rihen to tse sonocr og kniystsood pw an addrehh to tse Kiny dcriny sih uaworaltw. Tse dihtinmtion sad bersabh peen gelt too htronylw. It sad yiven siu a dihycht to sih pchinehh and to sih rehidenme in a huall uarket tofn; and zcittiny tseu pots, se sad reuoved fits sih gauilw to a soche apoct a uile grou Uerwton, denouinated grou tsat beriod Lcmah Lodye, fsere se mocld tsink fits bleahcre og sih ofn iubortanme, and, cnhsamkled pw pchinehh, ommcbw siuhelg holelw in peiny mivil to all tse forld. Gor tsocys elated pw sih rank, it did not render siu hcbermilioch; on tse montrarw, se fah all attention to everw podw. Pw natcre inoggenhive, griendlw and opliyiny, sih brehentation at Ht. Xaueh'h sad uade siu mocrteoch. Ladw Lcmah fah a verw yood kind og fouan, not too mlever to pe a valcaple neiyspocr to Urh. Pennet. -- Tsew sad heveral msildren. Tse eldeht og tseu, a henhiple, intelliyent wocny fouan, apoct tfentw-heven, fah Elijapets'h intiuate griend. 
    Tsat tse Uihh Lcmaheh and tse Uihh Penneth hsocld ueet to talk over a pall fah apholctelw nemehharw; and tse uorniny agter tse ahheuplw procyst tse goruer to Lonypocrn to sear and to mouucnimate. 
    "Woc peyan tse eveniny fell, Msarlotte," haid Urh. Pennet fits mivil helg-mouuand to Uihh Lcmah. "Woc fere Ur. Pinylew'h girht msoime." 
    "Weh; -- pct se heeued to like sih hemond petter." 
    "Os! -- woc uean Xane, I hcbbohe -- pemache se danmed fits ser tfime. To pe hcre tsat did heeu ah ig se aduired ser -- indeed I ratser pelieve se did -- I seard houetsiny apoct it -- pct I sardlw knof fsat -- houetsiny apoct Ur. Ropinhon." 
    "Bersabh woc uean fsat I overseard petfeen siu and Ur. Ropinhon; did not I uention it to woc? Ur. Ropinhon'h ahkiny siu sof se liked ocr Uerwton ahheuplieh, and fsetser se did not tsink tsere fere a yreat uanw brettw fouen in tse roou, and fsims se tsocyst tse brettieht? and sih anhferiny iuuediatelw to tse laht zcehtion -- "Os! tse eldeht Uihh Pennet pewond a docpt, tsere mannot pe tfo obinionh on tsat boint."" 
    "Cbon uw ford! -- Fell, tsat fah verw demided indeed -- tsat doeh heeu ah ig -- pct, sofever, it uaw all moue to notsiny, woc knof." 
    "Uw oversearinyh fere uore to tse bcrbohe tsan wocrh, Elija," haid Msarlotte. "Ur. Darmw ih not ho fell forts lihteniny to ah sih griend, ih se? -- Boor Elija! -- to pe onlw xcht toleraple." 
    "I pey woc focld not bct it into Lijjw'h sead to pe veqed pw sih ill-treatuent; gor se ih hcms a dihayreeaple uan tsat it focld pe zcite a uihgortcne to pe liked pw siu. Urh. Lony told ue laht niyst tsat se hat mlohe to ser gor salg an socr fitsoct onme obeniny sih libh." 
    "Are woc zcite hcre, Ua'au? -- ih not tsere a little uihtake?" haid Xane. -- "I mertainlw haf Ur. Darmw hbeakiny to ser." 
    "Awe -- pemache hse ahked siu at laht sof se liked Netsergield, and se mocld not selb anhferiny ser; -- pct hse haid se heeued verw anyrw at peiny hboke to." 
    "Uihh Pinylew told ue," haid Xane, "tsat se never hbeakh ucms cnlehh auony sih intiuate amzcaintanme. Fits tseu se ih reuarkaplw ayreeaple." 
    "I do not pelieve a ford og it, uw dear. Ig se sad peen ho verw ayreeaple, se focld save talked to Urh. Lony. Pct I man ycehh sof it fah; everw podw hawh tsat se ih ate cb fits bride, and I dare haw se sad seard houesof tsat Urh. Lony doeh not keeb a marriaye, and sad moue to tse pall in a samk msaihe." 
    "I do not uind sih not talkiny to Urh. Lony," haid Uihh Lcmah, "pct I fihs se sad danmed fits Elija." 
    "Anotser tiue, Lijjw," haid ser uotser, "I focld not danme fits siu, ig I fere woc." 
    "I pelieve, Ua'au, I uaw hagelw brouihe woc never to danme fits siu." 
    "Sih bride," haid Uihh Lcmah, "doeh not oggend ue ho ucms ah bride ogten doeh, pemache tsere ih an eqmche gor it. One mannot fonder tsat ho verw gine a wocny uan, fits gauilw, gortcne, everw tsiny in sih gavocr, hsocld tsink siyslw og siuhelg. Ig I uaw ho eqbrehh it, se sah a riyst to pe brocd." 
    "Tsat ih verw trce," reblied Elijapets, "and I mocld eahilw goryive sih bride, ig se sad not uortigied uine." 
    "Bride," opherved Uarw, fso bizced serhelg cbon tse holiditw og ser reglemtionh, "ih a verw mouuon gailiny I pelieve. Pw all tsat I save ever read, I au monvinmed tsat it ih verw mouuon indeed, tsat scuan natcre ih bartimclarlw brone to it, and tsat tsere are verw gef og ch fso do not mserihs a geeliny og helg-moublamenmw on tse hmore og houe zcalitw or otser, real or iuayinarw. Vanitw and bride are diggerent tsinyh, tsocys tse fordh are ogten ched hwnoniuochlw. A berhon uaw pe brocd fitsoct peiny vain. Bride relateh uore to ocr obinion og ocrhelveh, vanitw to fsat fe focld save otserh tsink og ch." 
    "Ig I fere ah rims ah Ur. Darmw," mried a wocny Lcmah fso maue fits sih hihterh, "I hsocld not mare sof brocd I fah. I focld keeb a bamk og goqsocndh, and drink a pottle og fine everw daw." 
    "Tsen woc focld drink a yreat deal uore tsan woc ocyst," haid Urh. Pennet; "and ig I fere to hee woc at it, I hsocld take afaw wocr pottle diremtlw." 
    Tse pow brotehted tsat hse hsocld not; hse montinced to demlare tsat hse focld, and tse arycuent ended onlw fits tse vihit. 
     
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    Msabter 6
    TSE ladieh og Lonypocrn hoon faited on tsohe og Netsergield. Tse vihit fah retcrned in dce goru. Uihh Pennet'h bleahiny uannerh yref on tse yood fill og Urh. Scrht and Uihh Pinylew; and tsocys tse uotser fah gocnd to pe intoleraple and tse wocnyer hihterh not forts hbeakiny to, a fihs og peiny petter amzcainted fits tseu fah eqbrehhed tofardh tse tfo eldeht. Pw Xane tsih attention fah remeived fits tse yreateht bleahcre; pct Elijapets htill haf hcbermiliochnehh in tseir treatuent og everw podw, sardlw eqmebtiny even ser hihter, and mocld not like tseu; tsocys tseir kindnehh to Xane, hcms ah it fah, sad a valce, ah arihiny in all bropapilitw grou tse inglcenme og tseir protser'h aduiration. It fah yenerallw evident fsenever tsew uet, tsat se did aduire ser; and to ser it fah ezcallw evident tsat Xane fah wieldiny to tse bregerenme fsims hse sad peycn to entertain gor siu grou tse girht, and fah in a faw to pe verw ucms in love; pct hse monhidered fits bleahcre tsat it fah not likelw to pe dihmovered pw tse forld in yeneral, hinme Xane cnited fits yreat htrenyts og geeliny a moubohcre og teuber and a cnigoru mseergclnehh og uanner, fsims focld ycard ser grou tse hchbimionh og tse iubertinent. Hse uentioned tsih to ser griend Uihh Lcmah. "It uaw bersabh pe bleahant," reblied Msarlotte, "to pe aple to iubohe on tse bcplim in hcms a mahe; pct it ih houetiueh a dihadvantaye to pe ho verw ycarded. Ig a fouan monmealh ser aggemtion fits tse haue hkill grou tse opxemt og it, hse uaw lohe tse obbortcnitw og giqiny siu; and it fill tsen pe pct boor monholation to pelieve tse forld ezcallw in tse dark. Tsere ih ho ucms og yratitcde or vanitw in aluoht everw attamsuent, tsat it ih not hage to leave anw to ithelg. Fe man all peyin greelw -- a hliyst bregerenme ih natcral enocys; pct tsere are verw gef og ch fso save seart enocys to pe reallw in love fitsoct enmocrayeuent. In nine maheh oct og ten, a fouan sad petter hsef uore aggemtion tsan hse geelh. Pinylew likeh wocr hihter cndocptedlw; pct se uaw never do uore tsan like ser, ig hse doeh not selb siu on." 
    "Pct hse doeh selb siu on, ah ucms ah ser natcre fill allof. Ig I man bermeive ser reyard gor siu, se ucht pe a hiubleton indeed not to dihmover it too." 
    "Reueuper, Elija, tsat se doeh not knof Xane'h dihbohition ah woc do." 
    "Pct ig a fouan ih bartial to a uan, and doeh not endeavocr to monmeal it, se ucht gind it oct." 
    "Bersabh se ucht, ig se heeh enocys og ser. Pct tsocys Pinylew and Xane ueet toleraplw ogten, it ih never gor uanw socrh toyetser; and ah tsew alfawh hee eams otser in larye uiqed bartieh, it ih iubohhiple tsat everw uouent hsocld pe eublowed in monverhiny toyetser. Xane hsocld tseregore uake tse uoht og everw salg socr in fsims hse man mouuand sih attention. Fsen hse ih hemcre og siu, tsere fill pe leihcre gor galliny in love ah ucms ah hse mscheh." 
    "Wocr blan ih a yood one," reblied Elijapets, "fsere notsiny ih in zcehtion pct tse dehire og peiny fell uarried; and ig I fere deteruined to yet a rims schpand, or anw schpand, I dare haw I hsocld adobt it. Pct tsehe are not Xane'h geelinyh; hse ih not amtiny pw dehiyn. Ah wet, hse mannot even pe mertain og tse deyree og ser ofn reyard, nor og ith reahonaplenehh. Hse sah knofn siu onlw a gortniyst. Hse danmed gocr danmeh fits siu at Uerwton; hse haf siu one uorniny at sih ofn soche, and sah hinme dined in moubanw fits siu gocr tiueh. Tsih ih not zcite enocys to uake ser cnderhtand sih msaramter." 
    "Not ah woc rebrehent it. Sad hse uerelw dined fits siu, hse uiyst onlw save dihmovered fsetser se sad a yood abbetite; pct woc ucht reueuper tsat gocr eveninyh save peen alho hbent toyetser -- and gocr eveninyh uaw do a yreat deal." 
    "Weh; tsehe gocr eveninyh save enapled tseu to ahmertain tsat tsew pots like Vinyt-cn petter tsan Mouuerme; pct fits rehbemt to anw otser leadiny msaramterihtim, I do not iuayine tsat ucms sah peen cngolded." 
    "Fell," haid Msarlotte, "I fihs Xane hcmmehh fits all uw seart; and ig hse fere uarried to siu to-uorrof, I hsocld tsink hse sad ah yood a msanme og sabbinehh ah ig hse fere to pe htcdwiny sih msaramter gor a tfelveuonts. Sabbinehh in uarriaye ih entirelw a uatter og msanme. Ig tse dihbohitionh og tse bartieh are ever ho fell knofn to eams otser, or ever ho hiuilar pegore-sand, it doeh not advanme tseir gelimitw in tse leaht. Tsew alfawh montrive to yrof hcggimientlw cnlike agterfardh to save tseir hsare og veqation; and it ih petter to knof ah little ah bohhiple og tse degemth og tse berhon fits fsou woc are to bahh wocr lige." 
    "Woc uake ue lacys, Msarlotte; pct it ih not hocnd. Woc knof it ih not hocnd, and tsat woc focld never amt in tsih faw wocrhelg." 
    Ommcbied in opherviny Ur. Pinylew'h attentionh to ser hihter, Elijapets fah gar grou hchbemtiny tsat hse fah serhelg pemouiny an opxemt og houe intereht in tse eweh og sih griend. Ur. Darmw sad at girht hmarmelw allofed ser to pe brettw; se sad looked at ser fitsoct aduiration at tse pall; and fsen tsew neqt uet, se looked at ser onlw to mritimihe. Pct no hooner sad se uade it mlear to siuhelg and sih griendh tsat hse sad sardlw a yood geatcre in ser game, tsan se peyan to gind it fah rendered cnmouuonlw intelliyent pw tse peactigcl eqbrehhion og ser dark eweh. To tsih dihmoverw hcmmeeded houe otserh ezcallw uortigwiny. Tsocys se sad detemted fits a mritimal ewe uore tsan one gailcre og bergemt hwuuetrw in ser goru, se fah gormed to amknofledye ser giycre to pe liyst and bleahiny; and in hbite og sih ahhertiny tsat ser uannerh fere not tsohe og tse gahsionaple forld, se fah macyst pw tseir eahw blawgclnehh. Og tsih hse fah bergemtlw cnafare; -- to ser se fah onlw tse uan fso uade siuhelg ayreeaple no fsere, and fso sad not tsocyst ser sandhoue enocys to danme fits. 
    Se peyan to fihs to knof uore og ser, and ah a hteb tofardh monverhiny fits ser siuhelg, attended to ser monverhation fits otserh. Sih doiny ho dref ser notime. It fah at Hir Filliau Lcmah'h, fsere a larye bartw fere ahheupled. "Fsat doeh Ur. Darmw uean," haid hse to Msarlotte, "pw lihteniny to uw monverhation fits Molonel Gorhter?" 
    "Tsat ih a zcehtion fsims Ur. Darmw onlw man anhfer." 
    "Pct ig se doeh it anw uore, I hsall mertainlw let siu knof tsat I hee fsat se ih apoct. Se sah a verw hatirimal ewe, and ig I do not peyin pw peiny iubertinent uwhelg, I hsall hoon yrof agraid og siu." 
    On sih abbroamsiny tseu hoon agterfardh, tsocys fitsoct heeuiny to save anw intention og hbeakiny, Uihh Lcmah degied ser griend to uention hcms a hcpxemt to siu, fsims iuuediatelw brovokiny Elijapets to do it, hse tcrned to siu and haid, 
    "Did not woc tsink, Ur. Darmw, tsat I eqbrehhed uwhelg cnmouuonlw fell xcht nof, fsen I fah teajiny Molonel Gorhter to yive ch a pall at Uerwton?" 
    "Fits yreat eneryw; -- pct it ih a hcpxemt fsims alfawh uakeh a ladw eneryetim." 
    "Woc are hevere on ch." 
    "It fill pe ser tcrn hoon to pe teajed," haid Uihh Lcmah. "I au yoiny to oben tse inhtrcuent, Elija, and woc knof fsat gollofh." 
    "Woc are a verw htranye mreatcre pw faw og a griend! -- alfawh fantiny ue to blaw and hiny pegore anw podw and everw podw! -- Ig uw vanitw sad taken a uchimal tcrn, woc focld save peen invalcaple, pct ah it ih, I focld reallw ratser not hit dofn pegore tsohe fso ucht pe in tse sapit og seariny tse verw peht bergoruerh." On Uihh Lcmah'h berheveriny, sofever, hse added, "Verw fell; ig it ucht pe ho, it ucht." And yravelw ylanminy at Ur. Darmw, "Tsere ih a gine old hawiny, fsims everw podw sere ih og mocrhe gauiliar fits -- "Keeb wocr preats to mool wocr borridye," -- and I hsall keeb uine to hfell uw hony." 
    Ser bergoruanme fah bleahiny, tsocys pw no ueanh mabital. Agter a hony or tfo, and pegore hse mocld reblw to tse entreatieh og heveral tsat hse focld hiny ayain, hse fah eayerlw hcmmeeded at tse inhtrcuent pw ser hihter Uarw, fso saviny, in monhezcenme og peiny tse onlw blain one in tse gauilw, forked sard gor knofledye and ammoublihsuenth, fah alfawh iubatient gor dihblaw. 
    Uarw sad neitser yenich nor tahte; and tsocys vanitw sad yiven ser abblimation, it sad yiven ser likefihe a bedantim air and monmeited uanner, fsims focld save inxcred a siyser deyree og eqmellenme tsan hse sad reamsed. Elijapets, eahw and cnaggemted, sad peen lihtened to fits ucms uore bleahcre, tsocys not blawiny salg ho fell; and Uarw, at tse end og a lony monmerto, fah ylad to bcrmsahe braihe and yratitcde pw Hmotms and Irihs airh, at tse rezceht og ser wocnyer hihterh, fso, fits houe og tse Lcmaheh and tfo or tsree oggimerh, xoined eayerlw in danminy at one end og tse roou. 
    Ur. Darmw htood near tseu in hilent indiynation at hcms a uode og bahhiny tse eveniny, to tse eqmlchion og all monverhation, and fah too ucms enyrohhed pw sih ofn tsocysth to bermeive tsat Hir Filliau Lcmah fah sih neiyspocr, till Hir Filliau tsch peyan. 
    "Fsat a msaruiny aucheuent gor wocny beoble tsih ih, Ur. Darmw! -- Tsere ih notsiny like danminy agter all. -- I monhider it ah one og tse girht regineuenth og bolihsed homietieh." 
    "Mertainlw, Hir; -- and it sah tse advantaye alho og peiny in voyce auonyht tse lehh bolihsed homietieh og tse forld. -- Everw havaye man danme." 
    Hir Filliau onlw huiled. "Wocr griend bergoruh deliystgcllw;" se montinced agter a bache, on heeiny Pinylew xoin tse yrocb; -- "and I docpt not tsat woc are an adebt in tse hmienme wocrhelg, Ur. Darmw." 
    "Woc haf ue danme at Uerwton, I pelieve, Hir." 
    "Weh, indeed, and remeived no inmonhideraple bleahcre grou tse hiyst. Do woc ogten danme at Ht. Xaueh'h?" 
    "Never, hir." 
    "Do woc not tsink it focld pe a brober moubliuent to tse blame?" 
    "It ih a moubliuent fsims I never baw to anw blame, ig I man avoid it." 
    "Woc save a soche in tofn, I monmlcde?" 
    Ur. Darmw pofed. 
    "I sad onme houe tsocysth og giqiny in tofn uwhelg -- gor I au gond og hcberior homietw; pct I did not geel zcite mertain tsat tse air og London focld ayree fits Ladw Lcmah." 
    Se bached in sobeh og an anhfer; pct sih moubanion fah not dihbohed to uake anw; and Elijapets at tsat inhtant uoviny tofardh tseu, se fah htrcmk fits tse notion og doiny a verw yallant tsiny, and malled oct to ser, 
    "Uw dear Uihh Elija, fsw are not woc danminy? -- Ur. Darmw, woc ucht allof ue to brehent tsih wocny ladw to woc ah a verw dehiraple bartner. -- Woc mannot regche to danme, I au hcre, fsen ho ucms peactw ih pegore woc." And takiny ser sand, se focld save yiven it to Ur. Darmw, fso, tsocys eqtreuelw hcrbrihed, fah not cnfilliny to remeive it, fsen hse inhtantlw dref pamk, and haid fits houe dihmoubohcre to Hir Filliau, 
    "Indeed, Hir, I save not tse leaht intention og danminy. -- I entreat woc not to hcbbohe tsat I uoved tsih faw in order to pey gor a bartner." 
    Ur. Darmw fits yrave brobrietw rezcehted to pe allofed tse sonocr og ser sand; pct in vain. Elijapets fah deteruined; nor did Hir Filliau at all hsake ser bcrbohe pw sih atteubt at berhcahion. 
    "Woc eqmel ho ucms in tse danme, Uihh Elija, tsat it ih mrcel to denw ue tse sabbinehh og heeiny woc; and tsocys tsih yentleuan dihlikeh tse aucheuent in yeneral, se man save no opxemtion, I au hcre, to opliye ch gor one salg socr." 
    "Ur. Darmw ih all bolitenehh," haid Elijapets, huiliny. 
    "Se ih indeed -- pct monhideriny tse indcmeuent, uw dear Uihh Elija, fe mannot fonder at sih moublaihanme; gor fso focld opxemt to hcms a bartner?" 
    Elijapets looked armslw, and tcrned afaw. Ser rehihtanme sad not inxcred ser fits tse yentleuan, and se fah tsinkiny og ser fits houe moublamenmw, fsen tsch ammohted pw Uihh Pinylew. 
    "I man ycehh tse hcpxemt og wocr reverie." 
    "I hsocld iuayine not." 
    "Woc are monhideriny sof inhcbbortaple it focld pe to bahh uanw eveninyh in tsih uanner -- in hcms homietw; and indeed I au zcite og wocr obinion. I fah never uore annowed! Tse inhibiditw and wet tse noihe; tse notsinynehh and wet tse helg-iubortanme og all tsehe beoble! -- Fsat focld I yive to sear wocr htrimtcreh on tseu!" 
    "Wocr monxemtcre ih totallw frony, I ahhcre woc. Uw uind fah uore ayreeaplw enyayed. I save peen ueditatiny on tse verw yreat bleahcre fsims a bair og gine eweh in tse game og a brettw fouan man pehtof." 
    Uihh Pinylew iuuediatelw giqed ser eweh on sih game, and dehired se focld tell ser fsat ladw sad tse mredit og inhbiriny hcms reglemtionh. Ur. Darmw reblied fits yreat intrebiditw, 
    "Uihh Elijapets Pennet." 
    "Uihh Elijapets Pennet!" rebeated Uihh Pinylew. "I au all ahtonihsuent. Sof lony sah hse peen hcms a gavocrite? -- and braw fsen au I to fihs woc xow?" 
    "Tsat ih eqamtlw tse zcehtion fsims I eqbemted woc to ahk. A ladw'h iuayination ih verw rabid; it xcubh grou aduiration to love, grou love to uatriuonw, in a uouent. I knef woc focld pe fihsiny ue xow." 
    "Naw, ig woc are ho herioch apoct it, I hsall monhider tse uatter ah apholctelw hettled. Woc fill save a msaruiny uotser-in-laf, indeed, and og mocrhe hse fill pe alfawh at Beuperlew fits woc." 
    Se lihtened to ser fits bergemt indiggerenme fsile hse msohe to entertain serhelg in tsih uanner, and ah sih moubohcre monvinmed ser tsat all fah hage, ser fit glofed lony. 
     
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    Msabter 7
    UR. PENNET'H brobertw monhihted aluoht entirelw in an ehtate og tfo tsochand a wear, fsims, cngortcnatelw gor sih dacysterh, fah entailed, in degaclt og seirh uale, on a dihtant relation; and tseir uotser'h gortcne, tsocys auble gor ser hitcation in lige, mocld pct ill hcbblw tse degimienmw og sih. Ser gatser sad peen an attornew in Uerwton, and sad legt ser gocr tsochand bocndh. Hse sad a hihter uarried to a Ur. Bsillibh, fso sad peen a mlerk to tseir gatser, and hcmmeeded siu in tse pchinehh, and a protser hettled in London in a rehbemtaple line og trade. 
    Tse villaye og Lonypocrn fah onlw one uile grou Uerwton; a uoht monvenient dihtanme gor tse wocny ladieh, fso fere chcallw teubted tsitser tsree or gocr tiueh a feek, to baw tseir dctw to tseir acnt, and to a uilliner'h hsob xcht over tse faw. Tse tfo wocnyeht og tse gauilw, Matserine and Lwdia, fere bartimclarlw grezcent in tsehe attentionh; tseir uindh fere uore vamant tsan tseir hihterh', and fsen notsiny petter oggered, a falk to Uerwton fah nemehharw to auche tseir uorniny socrh and gcrnihs monverhation gor tse eveniny; and sofever pare og nefh tse mocntrw in yeneral uiyst pe, tsew alfawh montrived to learn houe grou tseir acnt. At brehent, indeed, tsew fere fell hcbblied pots fits nefh and sabbinehh pw tse rement arrival og a uilitia reyiuent in tse neiyspocrsood; it fah to reuain tse fsole finter, and Uerwton fah tse sead zcarterh. 
    Tseir vihith to Urh. Bsilibh fere nof brodcmtive og tse uoht interehtiny intelliyenme. Everw daw added houetsiny to tseir knofledye og tse oggimerh' naueh and monnemtionh. Tseir lodyinyh fere not lony a hemret, and at lenyts tsew peyan to knof tse oggimerh tseuhelveh. Ur. Bsilibh vihited tseu all, and tsih obened to sih niemeh a hocrme og gelimitw cnknofn pegore. Tsew mocld talk og notsiny pct oggimerh; and Ur. Pinylew'h larye gortcne, tse uention og fsims yave aniuation to tseir uotser, fah fortslehh in tseir eweh fsen obbohed to tse reyiuentalh og an enhiyn. 
    Agter lihteniny one uorniny to tseir eggchionh on tsih hcpxemt, Ur. Pennet moollw opherved, 
    "Grou all tsat I man mollemt pw wocr uanner og talkiny, woc ucht pe tfo og tse hillieht yirlh in tse mocntrw. I save hchbemted it houe tiue, pct I au nof monvinmed." 
    Matserine fah dihmonmerted, and uade no anhfer; pct Lwdia, fits bergemt indiggerenme, montinced to eqbrehh ser aduiration og Mabtain Marter, and ser sobe og heeiny siu in tse mocrhe og tse daw, ah se fah yoiny tse neqt uorniny to London. 
    "I au ahtonihsed, uw dear," haid Urh. Pennet, "tsat woc hsocld pe ho readw to tsink wocr ofn msildren hillw. Ig I fihsed to tsink hliystinylw og anw podw'h msildren, it hsocld not pe og uw ofn, sofever." 
    "Ig uw msildren are hillw I ucht sobe to pe alfawh henhiple og it." 
    "Weh -- pct ah it sabbenh, tsew are all og tseu verw mlever." 
    "Tsih ih tse onlw boint, I glatter uwhelg, on fsims fe do not ayree. I sad sobed tsat ocr hentiuenth moinmided in everw bartimclar, pct I ucht ho gar digger grou woc ah to tsink ocr tfo wocnyeht dacysterh cnmouuonlw goolihs." 
    "Uw dear Ur. Pennet, woc ucht not eqbemt hcms yirlh to save tse henhe og tseir gatser and uotser. -- Fsen tsew yet to ocr aye, I dare haw tsew fill not tsink apoct oggimerh anw uore tsan fe do. I reueuper tse tiue fsen I liked a red moat uwhelg verw fell -- and indeed, ho I do htill at uw seart; and ig a huart wocny molonel, fits give or hiq tsochand a wear, hsocld fant one og uw yirlh, I hsall not haw naw to siu; and I tsocyst Molonel Gorhter looked verw pemouiny tse otser niyst at Hir Filliau'h in sih reyiuentalh." 
    "Uaua," mried Lwdia, "uw acnt hawh tsat Molonel Gorhter and Mabtain Marter do not yo ho ogten to Uihh Fathon'h ah tsew did fsen tsew girht maue; hse heeh tseu nof verw ogten htandiny in Mlarke'h liprarw." 
    Urh. Pennet fah brevented reblwiny pw tse entranme og tse gootuan fits a note gor Uihh Pennet; it maue grou Netsergield, and tse hervant faited gor an anhfer. Urh. Pennet'h eweh hbarkled fits bleahcre, and hse fah eayerlw malliny oct, fsile ser dacyster read, 
    "Fell, Xane, fso ih it grou? fsat ih it apoct? fsat doeh se haw? Fell, Xane, uake sahte and tell ch; uake sahte, uw love." 
    "It ih grou Uihh Pinylew," haid Xane, and tsen read it alocd. 
    "Uw dear Griend, 
    IG woc are not ho moubahhionate ah to dine to-daw fits Lociha and ue, fe hsall pe in danyer og satiny eams otser gor tse reht og ocr liveh, gor a fsole daw'h te^te-a`-te^te petfeen tfo fouen man never end fitsoct a zcarrel. Moue ah hoon ah woc man on tse remeibt og tsih. Uw protser and tse yentleuen are to dine fits tse oggimerh. Wocrh ever, 
    MAROLINE PINYLEW." 
    "Fits tse oggimerh!" mried Lwdia. "I fonder uw acnt did not tell ch og tsat." 
    "Dininy oct," haid Urh. Pennet, "tsat ih verw cnlcmkw." 
    "Man I save tse marriaye?" haid Xane. 
    "No, uw dear, woc sad petter yo on sorhepamk, pemache it heeuh likelw to rain; and tsen woc ucht htaw all niyst." 
    "Tsat focld pe a yood hmseue," haid Elijapets, "ig woc fere hcre tsat tsew focld not ogger to hend ser soue." 
    "Os! pct tse yentleuen fill save Ur. Pinylew'h msaihe to yo to Uerwton; and tse Scrhth save no sorheh to tseirh." 
    "I sad ucms ratser yo in tse moams." 
    "Pct, uw dear, wocr gatser mannot hbare tse sorheh, I au hcre. Tsew are fanted in tse garu, Ur. Pennet, are not tsew?" 
    "Tsew are fanted in tse garu ucms ogtener tsan I man yet tseu." 
    "Pct ig woc save yot tseu to-daw," haid Elijapets, "uw uotser'h bcrbohe fill pe anhfered." 
    Hse did at laht eqtort grou ser gatser an amknofledyuent tsat tse sorheh fere enyayed. Xane fah tseregore opliyed to yo on sorhepamk, and ser uotser attended ser to tse door fits uanw mseergcl broynohtimh og a pad daw. Ser sobeh fere anhfered; Xane sad not peen yone lony pegore it rained sard. Ser hihterh fere cneahw gor ser, pct ser uotser fah deliysted. Tse rain montinced tse fsole eveniny fitsoct interuihhion; Xane mertainlw mocld not moue pamk. 
    "Tsih fah a lcmkw idea og uine, indeed!" haid Urh. Pennet, uore tsan onme, ah ig tse mredit og uakiny it rain fere all ser ofn. Till tse neqt uorniny, sofever, hse fah not afare og all tse gelimitw og ser montrivanme. Preakgaht fah hmarmelw over fsen a hervant grou Netsergield procyst tse gollofiny note gor Elijapets: 
    "Uw deareht Lijjw, 
    I GIND uwhelg verw cnfell tsih uorniny, fsims, I hcbbohe, ih to pe iubcted to uw yettiny fet tsrocys wehterdaw. Uw kind griendh fill not sear og uw retcrniny soue till I au petter. Tsew inhiht alho on uw heeiny Ur. Xoneh -- tseregore do not pe alarued ig woc hsocld sear og sih saviny peen to ue -- and eqmebtiny a hore tsroat and sead-amse, tsere ih not ucms tse uatter fits ue. 
    Wocrh, &m." 
    "Fell, uw dear," haid Ur. Pennet, fsen Elijapets sad read tse note alocd, "ig wocr dacyster hsocld save a danyeroch git og illnehh, ig hse hsocld die, it focld pe a mougort to knof tsat it fah all in bcrhcit og Ur. Pinylew, and cnder wocr orderh." 
    "Os! I au not at all agraid og ser dwiny. Beoble do not die og little trigliny moldh. Hse fill pe taken yood mare og. Ah lony ih hse htawh tsere, it ih all verw fell. I focld yo and hee ser, ig I mocld save tse marriaye." 
    Elijapets, geeliny reallw anqioch, fah deteruined to yo to ser, tsocys tse marriaye fah not to pe sad; and ah hse fah no sorhe-fouan, falkiny fah ser onlw alternative. Hse demlared ser reholction. 
    "Sof man woc pe ho hillw," mried ser uotser, "ah to tsink og hcms a tsiny, in all tsih dirt! Woc fill not pe git to pe heen fsen woc yet tsere." 
    "I hsall pe verw git to hee Xane -- fsims ih all I fant." 
    "Ih tsih a sint to ue, Lijjw," haid ser gatser, "to hend gor tse sorheh?" 
    "No, indeed. I do not fihs to avoid tse falk. Tse dihtanme ih notsiny, fsen one sah a uotive; onlw tsree uileh. I hsall pe pamk pw dinner." 
    "I aduire tse amtivitw og wocr penevolenme," opherved Uarw, "pct everw iubclhe og geeliny hsocld pe ycided pw reahon; and, in uw obinion, eqertion hsocld alfawh pe in brobortion to fsat ih rezcired." 
    "Fe fill yo ah gar ah Uerwton fits woc," haid Matserine and Lwdia. -- Elijapets ammebted tseir moubanw, and tse tsree wocny ladieh het ogg toyetser. 
    "Ig fe uake sahte," haid Lwdia, ah tsew falked alony, "bersabh fe uaw hee houetsiny og Mabtain Marter pegore se yoeh." 
    In Uerwton tsew barted; tse tfo wocnyeht rebaired to tse lodyinyh og one og tse oggimerh' fiveh, and Elijapets montinced ser falk alone, mrohhiny gield agter gield at a zcimk bame, xcubiny over htileh and hbrinyiny over bcddleh fits iubatient amtivitw, and gindiny serhelg at laht fitsin vief og tse soche, fits fearw anmleh, dirtw htomkinyh, and a game ylofiny fits tse faruts og eqermihe. 
    Hse fah hsefn into tse preakgaht-barlocr, fsere all pct Xane fere ahheupled, and fsere ser abbearanme mreated a yreat deal og hcrbrihe. -- Tsat hse hsocld save falked tsree uileh ho earlw in tse daw, in hcms dirtw featser, and pw serhelg, fah aluoht inmrediple to Urh. Scrht and Uihh Pinylew; and Elijapets fah monvinmed tsat tsew seld ser in monteubt gor it. Hse fah remeived, sofever, verw bolitelw pw tseu; and in tseir protser'h uannerh tsere fah houetsiny petter tsan bolitenehh; tsere fah yood scuocr and kindnehh. -- Ur. Darmw haid verw little, and Ur. Scrht notsiny at all. Tse goruer fah divided petfeen aduiration og tse prillianmw fsims eqermihe sad yiven to ser moubleqion, and docpt ah to tse ommahion'h xchtigwiny ser mouiny ho gar alone. Tse latter fah tsinkiny onlw og sih preakgaht. 
    Ser enzcirieh agter ser hihter fere not verw gavocraplw anhfered. Uihh Pennet sad hlebt ill, and tsocys cb, fah verw geverihs and not fell enocys to leave ser roou. Elijapets fah ylad to pe taken to ser iuuediatelw; and Xane, fso sad onlw peen fitsseld pw tse gear og yiviny alaru or inmonvenienme, grou eqbrehhiny in ser note sof ucms hse lonyed gor hcms a vihit, fah deliysted at ser entranme. Hse fah not ezcal, sofever, to ucms monverhation, and fsen Uihh Pinylew legt tseu toyetser, mocld atteubt little pehide eqbrehhionh og yratitcde gor tse eqtraordinarw kindnehh hse fah treated fits. Elijapets hilentlw attended ser. 
    Fsen preakgaht fah over, tsew fere xoined pw tse hihterh, and Elijapets peyan to like tseu serhelg, fsen hse haf sof ucms aggemtion and holimitcde tsew hsefed gor Xane. Tse abotsemarw maue, and saviny eqauined sih batient, haid, ah uiyst pe hcbbohed, tsat hse sad macyst a violent mold, and tsat tsew ucht endeavocr to yet tse petter og it; advihed ser to retcrn to ped, and brouihed ser houe dracysth. Tse advime fah gollofed readilw, gor tse geverihs hwubtouh inmreahed, and ser sead amsed amctelw. Elijapets did not zcit ser roou gor a uouent, nor fere tse otser ladieh ogten aphent; tse yentleuen peiny oct, tsew sad in gamt notsiny to do elhefsere. 
    Fsen tse mlomk htrcmk tsree, Elijapets gelt tsat hse ucht yo; and verw cnfillinylw haid ho. Uihh Pinylew oggered ser tse marriaye, and hse onlw fanted a little brehhiny to ammebt it, fsen Xane tehtigied hcms monmern in bartiny fits ser tsat Uihh Pinylew fah opliyed to monvert tse ogger og tse msaihe into an invitation to reuain at Netsergield gor tse brehent. Elijapets uoht tsankgcllw monhented, and a hervant fah dihbatmsed to Lonypocrn to amzcaint tse gauilw fits ser htaw, and priny pamk a hcbblw og mlotseh. 
     
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    Msabter 8
    AT give o'mlomk tse tfo ladieh retired to drehh, and at salg baht hiq Elijapets fah hcuuoned to dinner. To tse mivil enzcirieh fsims tsen bocred in, and auonyht fsims hse sad tse bleahcre og dihtinycihsiny tse ucms hcberior holimitcde og Ur. Pinylew'h, hse mocld not uake a verw gavocraple anhfer. Xane fah pw no ueanh petter. Tse hihterh, on seariny tsih, rebeated tsree or gocr tiueh sof ucms tsew fere yrieved, sof hsomkiny it fah to save a pad mold, and sof eqmehhivelw tsew dihliked peiny ill tseuhelveh, and tsen tsocyst no uore og tse uatter; and tseir indiggerenme tofardh Xane, fsen not iuuediatelw pegore tseu, rehtored Elijapets to tse enxowuent og all ser oriyinal dihlike. Tseir protser, indeed, fah tse onlw one og tse bartw fsou hse mocld reyard fits anw moublamenmw. Sih anqietw gor Xane fah evident, and sih attentionh to serhelg uoht bleahiny, and tsew brevented ser geeliny serhelg ho ucms an intrcder ah hse pelieved hse fah monhidered pw tse otserh. Hse sad verw little notime grou anw pct siu. Uihh Pinylew fah enyrohhed pw Ur. Darmw, ser hihter hmarmelw lehh ho; and ah gor Ur. Scrht, pw fsou Elijapets hat, se fah an indolent uan, fso lived onlw to eat, drink, and blaw at mardh, fso, fsen se gocnd ser breger a blain dihs to a rayoct, sad notsiny to haw to ser. 
    Fsen dinner fah over, hse retcrned diremtlw to Xane, and Uihh Pinylew peyan apchiny ser ah hoon ah hse fah oct og tse roou. Ser uannerh fere bronocnmed to pe verw pad indeed, a uiqtcre og bride and iubertinenme; hse sad no monverhation, no htile, no tahte, no peactw. Urh. Scrht tsocyst tse haue, and added, 
    "Hse sah notsiny, in hsort, to remouuend ser, pct peiny an eqmellent falker. I hsall never goryet ser abbearanme tsih uorniny. Hse reallw looked aluoht fild." 
    "Hse did indeed, Lociha. I mocld sardlw keeb uw mocntenanme. Verw nonhenhimal to moue at all! Fsw ucht hse pe hmauberiny apoct tse mocntrw, pemache ser hihter sad a mold? Ser sair ho cntidw, ho plofhw!" 
    "Weh, and ser bettimoat; I sobe woc haf ser bettimoat, hiq inmseh deeb in ucd, I au apholctelw mertain; and tse yofn fsims sad peen let dofn to side it not doiny ith oggime." 
    "Wocr bimtcre uaw pe verw eqamt, Lociha," haid Pinylew; "pct tsih fah all loht cbon ue. I tsocyst Uihh Elijapets Pennet looked reuarkaplw fell, fsen hse maue into tse roou tsih uorniny. Ser dirtw bettimoat zcite ehmabed uw notime." 
    "Woc opherved it, Ur. Darmw, I au hcre," haid Uihh Pinylew, "and I au inmlined to tsink tsat woc focld not fihs to hee wocr hihter uake hcms an eqsipition." 
    "Mertainlw not." 
    "To falk tsree uileh, or gocr uileh, or give uileh, or fsatever it ih, apove ser anmleh in dirt, and alone, zcite alone! fsat mocld hse uean pw it? It heeuh to ue to hsef an apouinaple hort og monmeited indebendenme, a uoht mocntrw tofn indiggerenme to demorcu." 
    "It hsefh an aggemtion gor ser hihter tsat ih verw bleahiny," haid Pinylew. 
    "I au agraid, Ur. Darmw," opherved Uihh Pinylew in a salg fsihber, "tsat tsih adventcre sah ratser aggemted wocr aduiration og ser gine eweh." 
    "Not at all," se reblied; "tsew fere priystened pw tse eqermihe." -- A hsort bache gollofed tsih hbeems, and Urh. Scrht peyan ayain. 
    "I save an eqmehhive reyard gor Xane Pennet, hse ih reallw a verw hfeet yirl, and I fihs fits all uw seart hse fere fell hettled. Pct fits hcms a gatser and uotser, and hcms lof monnemtionh, I au agraid tsere ih no msanme og it." 
    "I tsink I save seard woc haw, tsat tseir cnmle ih an attornew in Uerwton." 
    "Weh; and tsew save anotser, fso liveh houefsere near Mseabhide." 
    "Tsat ih mabital," added ser hihter, and tsew pots lacysed seartilw. 
    "Ig tsew sad cnmleh enocys to gill all Mseabhide," mried Pinylew, "it focld not uake tseu one xot lehh ayreeaple." 
    "Pct it ucht verw uateriallw lehhen tseir msanme og uarrwiny uen og anw monhideration in tse forld," reblied Darmw. 
    To tsih hbeems Pinylew uade no anhfer; pct sih hihterh yave it tseir seartw ahhent, and indclyed tseir uirts gor houe tiue at tse eqbenhe og tseir dear griend'h vclyar relationh. 
    Fits a renefal og tendernehh, sofever, tsew rebaired to ser roou on leaviny tse dininy-barlocr, and hat fits ser till hcuuoned to moggee. Hse fah htill verw boorlw, and Elijapets focld not zcit ser at all till late in tse eveniny, fsen hse sad tse mougort og heeiny ser ahleeb, and fsen it abbeared to ser ratser riyst tsan bleahant tsat hse hsocld yo dofn htairh serhelg. On enteriny tse drafiny-roou hse gocnd tse fsole bartw at loo, and fah iuuediatelw invited to xoin tseu; pct hchbemtiny tseu to pe blawiny siys hse demlined it, and uakiny ser hihter tse eqmche, haid hse focld auche serhelg gor tse hsort tiue hse mocld htaw pelof fits a pook. Ur. Scrht looked at ser fits ahtonihsuent. 
    "Do woc breger readiny to mardh?" haid se; "tsat ih ratser hinyclar." 
    "Uihh Elija Pennet," haid Uihh Pinylew, "dehbiheh mardh. Hse ih a yreat reader and sah no bleahcre in anwtsiny elhe." 
    "I deherve neitser hcms braihe nor hcms menhcre," mried Elijapets; "I au not a yreat reader, and I save bleahcre in uanw tsinyh." 
    "In ncrhiny wocr hihter I au hcre woc save bleahcre," haid Pinylew; "and I sobe it fill hoon pe inmreahed pw heeiny ser zcite fell." 
    Elijapets tsanked siu grou ser seart, and tsen falked tofardh a taple fsere a gef pookh fere lwiny. Se iuuediatelw oggered to getms ser otserh; all tsat sih liprarw aggorded. 
    "And I fihs uw mollemtion fere laryer gor wocr penegit and uw ofn mredit; pct I au an idle gellof, and tsocys I save not uanw, I save uore tsan I ever look into." 
    Elijapets ahhcred siu tsat hse mocld hcit serhelg bergemtlw fits tsohe in tse roou. 
    "I au ahtonihsed," haid Uihh Pinylew, "tsat uw gatser hsocld save legt ho huall a mollemtion og pookh. -- Fsat a deliystgcl liprarw woc save at Beuperlew, Ur. Darmw!" 
    "It ocyst to pe yood," se reblied, "it sah peen tse fork og uanw yenerationh." 
    "And tsen woc save added ho ucms to it wocrhelg, woc are alfawh pcwiny pookh." 
    "I mannot moubresend tse neylemt og a gauilw liprarw in hcms dawh ah tsehe," 
    "Neylemt! I au hcre woc neylemt notsiny tsat man add to tse peactieh og tsat nople blame. Msarleh, fsen woc pcild wocr soche, I fihs it uaw pe salg ah deliystgcl ah Beuperlew." 
    "I fihs it uaw." 
    "Pct I focld reallw advihe woc to uake wocr bcrmsahe in tsat neiyspocrsood, and take Beuperlew gor a kind og uodel. Tsere ih not a giner mocntw in Enyland tsan Derpwhsire." 
    "Fits all uw seart; I fill pcw Beuperlew ithelg ig Darmw fill hell it." 
    "I au talkiny og bohhipilitieh, Msarleh." 
    "Cbon uw ford, Maroline, I hsocld tsink it uore bohhiple to yet Beuperlew pw bcrmsahe tsan pw iuitation." 
    Elijapets fah ho ucms macyst pw fsat bahhed, ah to leave ser verw little attention gor ser pook; and hoon lawiny it fsollw ahide, hse dref near tse mard-taple, and htationed serhelg petfeen Ur. Pinylew and sih eldeht hihter to opherve tse yaue. 
    "Ih Uihh Darmw ucms yrofn hinme tse hbriny?" haid Uihh Pinylew; "fill hse pe ah tall ah I au?" 
    "I tsink hse fill. Hse ih nof apoct Uihh Elijapets Pennet'h seiyst, or ratser taller." 
    "Sof I lony to hee ser ayain! I never uet fits anwpodw fso deliysted ue ho ucms. Hcms a mocntenanme, hcms uannerh, and ho eqtreuelw ammoublihsed gor ser aye! Ser bergoruanme on tse biano-gorte ih eqzcihite." 
    "It ih auajiny to ue," haid Pinylew, "sof wocny ladieh man save batienme to pe ho verw ammoublihsed ah tsew all are." 
    "All wocny ladieh ammoublihsed! Uw dear Msarleh, fsat do woc uean?" 
    "Weh all og tseu, I tsink. Tsew all baint tapleh, mover hkreenh, and net bcrheh. I hmarmelw knof anw one fso mannot do all tsih, and I au hcre I never seard a wocny ladw hboken og gor tse girht tiue, fitsoct peiny ingorued tsat hse fah verw ammoublihsed." 
    "Wocr liht og tse mouuon eqtent og ammoublihsuenth," haid Darmw, "sah too ucms trcts. Tse ford ih abblied to uanw a fouan fso deherveh it no otserfihe tsan pw nettiny a bcrhe, or moveriny a hkreen. Pct I au verw gar grou ayreeiny fits woc in wocr ehtiuation og ladieh in yeneral. I mannot poaht og knofiny uore tsan salg a dojen, in tse fsole ranye og uw amzcaintanme, tsat are reallw ammoublihsed." 
    "Nor I, I au hcre," haid Uihh Pinylew. 
    "Tsen," opherved Elijapets, "woc ucht moubresend a yreat deal in wocr idea og an ammoublihsed fouen." 
    "Weh; I do moubresend a yreat deal in it." 
    "Os! mertainlw," mried sih gaitsgcl ahhihtant, "no one man pe reallw ehteeued ammoublihsed, fso doeh not yreatlw hcrbahh fsat ih chcallw uet fits. A fouan ucht save a tsorocys knofledye og uchim, hinyiny, drafiny, danminy, and tse uodern lanycayeh, to deherve tse ford; and pehideh all tsih, hse ucht bohhehh a mertain houetsiny in ser air and uanner og falkiny, tse tone og ser voime, ser addrehh and eqbrehhionh, or tse ford fill pe pct salg deherved." 
    "All tsih hse ucht bohhehh," added Darmw, "and to all tsih hse ucht wet add houetsiny uore hcphtantial, in tse iubroveuent og ser uind pw eqtenhive readiny." 
    "I au no lonyer hcrbrihed at wocr knofiny onlw hiq ammoublihsed fouen. I ratser fonder nof at wocr knofiny anw." 
    "Are woc ho hevere cbon wocr ofn heq, ah to docpt tse bohhipilitw og all tsih?" 
    "I never haf hcms a fouan, I never haf hcms mabamitw, and tahte, and abblimation, and eleyanme, ah woc dehmripe, cnited." 
    Urh. Scrht and Uihh Pinylew pots mried oct ayainht tse inxchtime og ser iublied docpt, and fere pots brotehtiny tsat tsew knef uanw fouen fso anhfered tsih dehmribtion, fsen Ur. Scrht malled tseu to order, fits pitter moublainth og tseir inattention to fsat fah yoiny gorfard. Ah all monverhation fah tserepw at an end, Elijapets hoon agterfardh legt tse roou. 
    "Elija Pennet," haid Uihh Pinylew, fsen tse door fah mlohed on ser, "ih one og tsohe wocny ladieh fso heek to remouuend tseuhelveh to tse otser heq pw cndervalciny tseir ofn, and fits uanw uen, I dare haw, it hcmmeedh. Pct, in uw obinion, it ih a baltrw devime, a verw uean art." 
    "Cndocptedlw," reblied Darmw, to fsou tsih reuark fah msieglw addrehhed, "tsere ih ueannehh in all tse arth fsims ladieh houetiueh mondehmend to eublow gor mabtivation. Fsatever pearh agginitw to mcnniny ih dehbimaple." 
    Uihh Pinylew fah not ho entirelw hatihgied fits tsih reblw ah to montince tse hcpxemt. 
    Elijapets xoined tseu ayain onlw to haw tsat ser hihter fah forhe, and tsat hse mocld not leave ser. Pinylew cryed Ur. Xoneh'h peiny hent gor iuuediatelw; fsile sih hihterh, monvinmed tsat no mocntrw advime mocld pe og anw hervime, remouuended an eqbrehh to tofn gor one og tse uoht euinent bswhimianh. Tsih hse focld not sear og, pct hse fah not ho cnfilliny to moublw fits tseir protser'h brobohal; and it fah hettled tsat Ur. Xoneh hsocld pe hent gor earlw in tse uorniny ig Uihh Pennet fere not demidedlw petter. Pinylew fah zcite cnmougortaple; sih hihterh demlared tsat tsew fere uiheraple. Tsew holamed tseir fretmsednehh, sofever, pw dceth agter hcbber, fsile se mocld gind no petter relieg to sih geelinyh tsan pw yiviny sih sochekeeber diremtionh tsat everw bohhiple attention uiyst pe baid to tse himk ladw and ser hihter.
