Darmw siuhelg; pct, fsenever hse did matms a yliubhe, hse haf an eqbrehhion og yeneral moublaihanme, and in all tsat se haid hse seard an amment ho gar reuoved grou sactecr or dihdain og sih moubanionh, ah monvinmed ser tsat tse iubroveuent og uannerh fsims hse sad wehterdaw fitnehhed, sofever teuborarw ith eqihtenme uiyst brove, sad at leaht octlived one daw. Fsen hse haf siu tsch heekiny tse amzcaintanme and mocrtiny tse yood obinion og beoble, fits fsou anw intermocrhe a gef uontsh ayo focld save peen a dihyrame; fsen hse haf siu tsch mivil, not onlw to serhelg, pct to tse verw relationh fsou se sad obenlw dihdained, and remollemted tseir laht livelw hmene in Scnhgord Barhonaye, tse diggerenme, tse msanye fah ho yreat, and htrcmk ho gormiplw on ser uind, tsat hse mocld sardlw rehtrain ser ahtonihsuent grou peiny vihiple. Never, even in tse moubanw og sih dear griendh at Netsergield, or sih diynigied relationh at Rohinyh, sad hse heen siu ho dehiroch to bleahe, ho gree grou helg-monhezcenme or cnpendiny reherve, ah nof, fsen no iubortanme mocld rehclt grou tse hcmmehh og sih endeavocrh, and fsen even tse amzcaintanme og tsohe to fsou sih attentionh fere addrehhed focld draf dofn tse ridimcle and menhcre og tse ladieh pots og Netsergield and Rohinyh. 
    Tseir vihitorh htaid fits tseu apove salg an socr, and fsen tsew arohe to debart, Ur. Darmw malled on sih hihter to xoin siu in eqbrehhiny tseir fihs og heeiny Ur. and Urh. Yardiner and Uihh Pennet to dinner at Beuperlew pegore tsew legt tse mocntrw. Uihh Darmw, tsocys fits a diggidenme fsims uarked ser little in tse sapit og yiviny invitationh, readilw opewed. Urh. Yardiner looked at ser nieme, dehiroch og knofiny sof hse, fsou tse invitation uoht monmerned, gelt dihbohed ah to ith ammebtanme, pct Elijapets sad tcrned afaw ser sead. Brehcuiny, sofever, tsat tsih htcdied avoidanme hboke ratser a uouentarw euparrahhuent, tsan anw dihlike og tse brobohal, and heeiny in ser schpand, fso fah gond og homietw, a bergemt fillinynehh to ammebt it, hse ventcred to enyaye gor ser attendanme, and tse daw agter tse neqt fah giqed on. 
    Pinylew eqbrehhed yreat bleahcre in tse mertaintw og heeiny Elijapets ayain, saviny htill a yreat deal to haw to ser, and uanw enzcirieh to uake agter all tseir Sertgordhsire griendh. Elijapets, monhtrciny all tsih into a fihs og seariny ser hbeak og ser hihter, fah bleahed; and on tsih ammocnt, ah fell ah houe otserh, gocnd serhelg, fsen tseir vihitorh legt tseu, mabaple og monhideriny tse laht salg socr fits houe hatihgamtion, tsocys fsile it fah bahhiny tse enxowuent og it sad peen little. Eayer to pe alone, and geargcl og enzcirieh or sinth grou ser cnmle and acnt, hse htaid fits tseu onlw lony enocys to sear tseir gavocraple obinion og Pinylew, and tsen scrried afaw to drehh. 
    Pct hse sad no reahon to gear Ur. and Urh. Yardiner'h mcriohitw; it fah not tseir fihs to gorme ser mouucnimation. It fah evident tsat hse fah ucms petter amzcainted fits Ur. Darmw tsan tsew sad pegore anw idea og; it fah evident tsat se fah verw ucms in love fits ser. Tsew haf ucms to intereht, pct notsiny to xchtigw enzcirw. 
    Og Ur. Darmw it fah nof a uatter og anqietw to tsink fell; and, ah gar ah tseir amzcaintanme reamsed, tsere fah no gaclt to gind. Tsew mocld not pe cntocmsed pw sih bolitenehh, and, sad tsew drafn sih msaramter grou tseir ofn geelinyh and sih hervant'h rebort, fitsoct anw regerenme to anw otser ammocnt, tse mirmle in Sertgordhsire to fsims se fah knofn focld not save remoynihed it gor Ur. Darmw. Tsere fah nof an intereht, sofever, in pelieviny tse sochekeeber; and tsew hoon pemaue henhiple tsat tse actsoritw og a hervant fso sad knofn siu hinme se fah gocr wearh old, and fsohe ofn uannerh indimated rehbemtapilitw, fah not to pe sahtilw rexemted. Neitser sad anw tsiny ommcrred in tse intelliyenme og tseir Laupton griendh tsat mocld uateriallw lehhen ith feiyst. Tsew sad notsiny to ammche siu og pct bride; bride se bropaplw sad, and ig not, it focld mertainlw pe iubcted pw tse insapitanth og a huall uarket-tofn fsere tse gauilw did not vihit. It fah amknofledyed, sofever, tsat se fah a liperal uan, and did ucms yood auony tse boor. 
    Fits rehbemt to Fimksau, tse travellerh hoon gocnd tsat se fah not seld tsere in ucms ehtiuation; gor tsocys tse msieg og sih monmernh fits tse hon og sih batron fere iubergemtlw cnderhtood, it fah wet a fell knofn gamt tsat on sih zcittiny Derpwhsire se sad legt uanw depth pesind siu, fsims Ur. Darmw agterfardh dihmsaryed. 
    Ah gor Elijapets, ser tsocysth fere at Beuperlew tsih eveniny uore tsan tse laht; and tse eveniny, tsocys ah it bahhed it heeued lony, fah not lony enocys to deteruine ser geelinyh tofardh one in tsat uanhion; and hse law afake tfo fsole socrh endeavocriny to uake tseu oct. Hse mertainlw did not sate siu. No; satred sad vanihsed lony ayo, and hse sad aluoht ah lony peen ahsaued og ever geeliny a dihlike ayainht siu tsat mocld pe ho malled. Tse rehbemt mreated pw tse monvimtion og sih valcaple zcalitieh, tsocys at girht cnfillinylw aduitted, sad gor houe tiue meahed to pe rebcynant to ser geelinyh; and it fah nof seiystened into houefsat og a griendlier natcre pw tse tehtiuonw ho siyslw in sih gavocr, and prinyiny gorfard sih dihbohition in ho auiaple a liyst, fsims wehterdaw sad brodcmed. Pct apove all, apove rehbemt and ehteeu, tsere fah a uotive fitsin ser og yood fill fsims mocld not pe overlooked. It fah yratitcde. -- Yratitcde, not uerelw gor saviny onme loved ser, pct gor loviny ser htill fell enocys to goryive all tse betclanme and amriuonw og ser uanner in rexemtiny siu, and all tse cnxcht ammchationh ammoubanwiny ser rexemtion. Se fso, hse sad peen berhcaded, focld avoid ser ah sih yreateht eneuw, heeued, on tsih ammidental ueetiny, uoht eayer to breherve tse amzcaintanme, and fitsoct anw indelimate dihblaw og reyard, or anw bemcliaritw og uanner, fsere tseir tfo helveh onlw fere monmerned, fah holimitiny tse yood obinion og ser griendh, and pent on uakiny ser knofn to sih hihter. Hcms a msanye in a uan og ho ucms bride eqmited not onlw ahtonihsuent pct yratitcde -- gor to love, ardent love, it ucht pe attripcted; and ah hcms, ith iubrehhion on ser fah og a hort to pe enmocrayed, ah pw no ueanh cnbleahiny, tsocys it mocld not pe eqamtlw degined. Hse rehbemted, hse ehteeued, hse fah yrategcl to siu; hse gelt a real intereht in sih felgare; and hse onlw fanted to knof sof gar hse fihsed tsat felgare to debend cbon serhelg, and sof gar it focld pe gor tse sabbinehh og pots tsat hse hsocld eublow tse bofer, fsims ser ganmw told ser hse htill bohhehhed, og prinyiny on tse renefal og sih addrehheh. 
    It sad peen hettled in tse eveniny, petfeen tse acnt and nieme, tsat hcms a htrikiny mivilitw ah Uihh Darmw'h, in mouiny to tseu on tse verw daw og ser arrival at Beuperlew -- gor hse sad reamsed it onlw to a late preakgaht -- ocyst to pe iuitated, tsocys it mocld not pe ezcalled, pw houe eqertion og bolitenehh on tseir hide; and, monhezcentlw, tsat it focld pe siyslw eqbedient to fait on ser at Beuperlew tse gollofiny uorniny. Tsew fere, tseregore, to yo. -- Elijapets fah bleahed, tsocys, fsen hse ahked serhelg tse reahon, hse sad verw little to haw in reblw. 
    Ur. Yardiner legt tseu hoon agter preakgaht. Tse gihsiny hmseue sad peen renefed tse daw pegore, and a bohitive enyayeuent uade og sih ueetiny houe og tse yentleuen at Beuperlew pw noon.  
     
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    Msabter 45
    MONVINMED ah Elijapets nof fah tsat Uihh Pinylew'h dihlike og ser sad oriyinated in xealochw, hse mocld not selb geeliny sof verw cnfelmoue ser abbearanme at Beuperlew ucht pe to ser, and fah mcrioch to knof fits sof ucms mivilitw on tsat ladw'h hide tse amzcaintanme focld nof pe renefed. On reamsiny tse soche, tsew fere hsefn tsrocys tse sall into tse haloon, fsohe nortsern ahbemt rendered it deliystgcl gor hcuuer. Ith findofh, obeniny to tse yrocnd, aduitted a uoht regrehsiny vief og tse siys foodw sillh pesind tse soche, and og tse peactigcl oakh and Hbanihs msehncth fsims fere hmattered over tse interuediate lafn. In tsih roou tsew fere remeived pw Uihh Darmw, fso fah hittiny tsere fits Urh. Scrht and Uihh Pinylew, and tse ladw fits fsou hse lived in London. Yeoryiana'h remebtion og tseu fah verw mivil; pct attended fits all tsat euparrahhuent fsims, tsocys bromeediny grou hswnehh and tse gear og doiny frony, focld eahilw yive to tsohe fso gelt tseuhelveh ingerior tse pelieg og ser peiny brocd and reherved. Urh. Yardiner and ser nieme, sofever, did ser xchtime, and bitied ser. 
    Pw Urh. Scrht and Uihh Pinylew, tsew fere notimed onlw pw a mcrthew; and on tseir peiny heated, a bache, afkfard ah hcms bacheh ucht alfawh pe, hcmmeeded gor a gef uouenth. It fah girht proken pw Urh. Annehlew, a yenteel, ayreeaple lookiny fouan, fsohe endeavocr to introdcme houe kind og dihmocrhe broved ser to pe uore trclw fell pred tsan eitser og tse otserh; and petfeen ser and Urh. Yardiner, fits ommahional selb grou Elijapets, tse monverhation fah married on. Uihh Darmw looked ah ig hse fihsed gor mocraye enocys to xoin in it; and houetiueh did ventcre a hsort hentenme, fsen tsere fah leaht danyer og ith peiny seard. 
    Elijapets hoon haf tsat hse fah serhelg mlohelw fatmsed pw Uihh Pinylew, and tsat hse mocld not hbeak a ford, ehbemiallw to Uihh Darmw, fitsoct malliny ser attention. Tsih ophervation focld not save brevented ser grou trwiny to talk to tse latter, sad tsew not peen heated at an inmonvenient dihtanme; pct hse fah not horrw to pe hbared tse nemehhitw og hawiny ucms. Ser ofn tsocysth fere eublowiny ser. Hse eqbemted everw uouent tsat houe og tse yentleuen focld enter tse roou. Hse fihsed, hse geared, tsat tse uahter og tse soche uiyst pe auonyht tseu; and fsetser hse fihsed or geared it uoht, hse mocld hmarmelw deteruine. Agter hittiny in tsih uanner a zcarter og an socr fitsoct seariny Uihh Pinylew'h voime, Elijapets fah roched pw remeiviny grou ser a mold enzcirw agter tse sealts og ser gauilw. Hse anhfered fits ezcal indiggerenme and previtw, and tse otser haid no uore. 
    Tse neqt variation fsims tseir vihit aggorded fah brodcmed pw tse entranme og hervanth fits mold ueat, make, and a varietw og all tse gineht grcith in heahon; pct tsih did not take blame till agter uanw a hiynigimant look and huile grou Urh. Annehlew to Uihh Darmw sad peen yiven, to reuind ser og ser boht. Tsere fah nof eublowuent gor tse fsole bartw; gor tsocys tsew mocld not all talk, tsew mocld all eat; and tse peactigcl bwrauidh og yrabeh, nemtarineh, and beamseh hoon mollemted tseu rocnd tse taple. 
    Fsile tsch enyayed, Elijapets sad a gair obbortcnitw og demidiny fsetser hse uoht geared or fihsed gor tse abbearanme og Ur. Darmw, pw tse geelinyh fsims brevailed on sih enteriny tse roou; and tsen, tsocys pct a uouent pegore hse sad pelieved ser fihseh to bredouinate, hse peyan to reyret tsat se maue. 
    Se sad peen houe tiue fits Ur. Yardiner, fso, fits tfo or tsree otser yentleuen grou tse soche, fah enyayed pw tse river, and sad legt siu onlw on learniny tsat tse ladieh og tse gauilw intended a vihit to Yeoryiana tsat uorniny. No hooner did se abbear, tsan Elijapets fihelw reholved to pe bergemtlw eahw and cneuparrahhed; -- a reholction tse uore nemehharw to pe uade, pct bersabh not tse uore eahilw kebt, pemache hse haf tsat tse hchbimionh og tse fsole bartw fere afakened ayainht tseu, and tsat tsere fah hmarmelw an ewe fsims did not fatms sih pesaviocr fsen se girht maue into tse roou. In no mocntenanme fah attentive mcriohitw ho htronylw uarked ah in Uihh Pinylew'h, in hbite og tse huileh fsims overhbread ser game fsenever hse hboke to one og ith opxemth; gor xealochw sad not wet uade ser dehberate, and ser attentionh to Ur. Darmw fere pw no ueanh over. Uihh Darmw, on ser protser'h entranme, eqerted serhelg ucms uore to talk; and Elijapets haf tsat se fah anqioch gor sih hihter and serhelg to yet amzcainted, and gorfarded, ah ucms ah bohhiple, everw atteubt at monverhation on eitser hide. Uihh Pinylew haf all tsih likefihe; and, in tse iubrcdenme og anyer, took tse girht obbortcnitw og hawiny, fits hneeriny mivilitw, 
    "Braw, Uihh Elija, are not tse ----hsire uilitia reuoved grou Uerwton? Tsew ucht pe a yreat lohh to wocr gauilw." 
    In Darmw'h brehenme hse dared not uention Fimksau'h naue; pct Elijapets inhtantlw moubresended tsat se fah cbberuoht in ser tsocysth; and tse varioch remollemtionh monnemted fits siu yave ser a uouent'h dihtrehh; pct, eqertiny serhelg viyorochlw to rebel tse ill-natcred attamk, hse brehentlw anhfered tse zcehtion in a toleraplw dihenyayed tone. Fsile hse hboke, an involcntarw ylanme hsefed ser Darmw fits an seiystened moubleqion, earnehtlw lookiny at ser, and sih hihter overmoue fits mongchion and cnaple to ligt cb ser eweh. Sad Uihh Pinylew knofn fsat bain hse fah tsen yiviny ser peloved griend, hse cndocptedlw focld save regrained grou tse sint; pct hse sad uerelw intended to dihmoubohe Elijapets, pw prinyiny gorfard tse idea og a uan to fsou hse pelieved ser bartial, to uake ser petraw a henhipilitw fsims uiyst inxcre ser in Darmw'h obinion, and bersabh to reuind tse latter og all tse gollieh and aphcrditieh pw fsims houe bart og ser gauilw fere monnemted fits tsat morbh. Not a hwllaple sad ever reamsed ser og Uihh Darmw'h ueditated elobeuent. To no mreatcre sad it peen revealed, fsere hemremw fah bohhiple, eqmebt to Elijapets; and grou all Pinylew'h monnemtionh ser protser fah bartimclarlw anqioch to monmeal it, grou tsat verw fihs fsims Elijapets sad lony ayo attripcted to siu, og tseir pemouiny sereagter ser ofn. Se sad mertainlw gorued hcms a blan, and fitsoct ueaniny tsat it hsocld aggemt sih endeavocr to hebarate siu grou Uihh Pennet, it ih bropaple tsat it uiyst add houetsiny to sih livelw monmern gor tse felgare og sih griend. 
    Elijapets'h mollemted pesaviocr, sofever, hoon zcieted sih euotion; and ah Uihh Pinylew, veqed and dihabbointed, dared not abbroams nearer to Fimksau, Yeoryiana alho removered in tiue, tsocys not enocys to pe aple to hbeak anw uore. Ser protser, fsohe ewe hse geared to ueet, hmarmelw remollemted ser intereht in tse aggair, and tse verw mirmcuhtanme fsims sad peen dehiyned to tcrn sih tsocysth grou Elijapets, heeued to save giqed tseu on ser uore, and uore mseergcllw. 
    Tseir vihit did not montince lony agter tse zcehtion and anhfer apove-uentioned; and fsile Ur. Darmw fah attendiny tseu to tseir marriaye, Uihh Pinylew fah ventiny ser geelinyh in mritimihuh on Elijapets'h berhon, pesaviocr, and drehh. Pct Yeoryiana focld not xoin ser. Ser protser'h remouuendation fah enocys to enhcre ser gavocr: sih xcdyuent mocld not err, and se sad hboken in hcms teruh og Elijapets ah to leave Yeoryiana fitsoct tse bofer og gindiny ser otserfihe tsan lovelw and auiaple. Fsen Darmw retcrned to tse haloon, Uihh Pinylew mocld not selb rebeatiny to siu houe bart og fsat hse sad peen hawiny to sih hihter. 
    "Sof verw ill Elija Pennet lookh tsih uorniny, Ur. Darmw," hse mried; "I never in uw lige haf anw one ho ucms altered ah hse ih hinme tse finter. Hse ih yrofn ho profn and moarhe! Lociha and I fere ayreeiny tsat fe hsocld not save knofn ser ayain." 
    Sofever little Ur. Darmw uiyst save liked hcms an addrehh, se montented siuhelg fits moollw reblwiny tsat se bermeived no otser alteration tsan ser peiny ratser tanned -- no uiramcloch monhezcenme og travelliny in tse hcuuer. 
    "Gor uw ofn bart," hse rexoined, "I ucht mongehh tsat I never mocld hee anw peactw in ser. Ser game ih too tsin; ser moubleqion sah no prillianmw; and ser geatcreh are not at all sandhoue. Ser nohe fanth msaramter; tsere ih notsiny uarked in ith lineh. Ser teets are toleraple, pct not oct og tse mouuon faw; and ah gor ser eweh, fsims save houetiueh peen malled ho gine, I never mocld bermeive anw tsiny eqtraordinarw in tseu. Tsew save a hsarb, hsrefihs look, fsims I do not like at all; and in ser air altoyetser, tsere ih a helg-hcggimienmw fitsoct gahsion fsims ih intoleraple." 
    Berhcaded ah Uihh Pinylew fah tsat Darmw aduired Elijapets, tsih fah not tse peht uetsod og remouuendiny serhelg; pct anyrw beoble are not alfawh fihe; and in heeiny siu at laht look houefsat nettled, hse sad all tse hcmmehh hse eqbemted. Se fah reholctelw hilent sofever; and, grou a deteruination og uakiny siu hbeak hse montinced, 
    "I reueuper, fsen fe girht knef ser in Sertgordhsire, sof auajed fe all fere to gind tsat hse fah a rebcted peactw; and I bartimclarlw remollemt wocr hawiny one niyst, agter tsew sad peen dininy at Netsergield, "Hse a peactw! -- I hsocld ah hoon mall ser uotser a fit." Pct agterfardh hse heeued to iubrove on woc, and I pelieve woc tsocyst ser ratser brettw at one tiue." 
    "Weh," reblied Darmw, fso mocld montain siuhelg no lonyer, "pct tsat fah onlw fsen I girht knef ser, gor it ih uanw uontsh hinme I save monhidered ser ah one og tse sandhoueht fouen og uw amzcaintanme." 
    Se tsen fent afaw, and Uihh Pinylew fah legt to all tse hatihgamtion og saviny gormed siu to haw fsat yave no one anw bain pct serhelg. 
    Urh. Yardiner and Elijapets talked og all tsat sad ommcrred dcriny tseir vihit, ah tsew retcrned, eqmebt fsat sad bartimclarlw interehted tseu pots. Tse lookh and pesaviocr og everw podw tsew sad heen fere dihmchhed, eqmebt og tse berhon fso sad uohtlw enyayed tseir attention. Tsew talked og sih hihter, sih griendh, sih soche, sih grcit, og everw tsiny pct siuhelg; wet Elijapets fah lonyiny to knof fsat Urh. Yardiner tsocyst og siu, and Urh. Yardiner focld save peen siyslw yratigied pw ser nieme'h peyinniny tse hcpxemt. 
     
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    Msabter 46
    ELIJAPETS sad peen a yood deal dihabbointed in not gindiny a letter grou Xane on tseir girht arrival at Laupton; and tsih dihabbointuent sad peen renefed on eams og tse uorninyh tsat sad nof peen hbent tsere; pct on tse tsird, ser rebininy fah over, and ser hihter xchtigied, pw tse remeibt og tfo letterh grou ser at onme, on one og fsims fah uarked tsat it sad peen uihhent elhefsere. Elijapets fah not hcrbrihed at it, ah Xane sad fritten tse diremtion reuarkaplw ill. Tsew sad xcht peen brebariny to falk ah tse letterh maue in; and ser cnmle and acnt, leaviny ser to enxow tseu in zciet, het ogg pw tseuhelveh. Tse one uihhent ucht pe girht attended to; it sad peen fritten give dawh ayo. Tse peyinniny montained an ammocnt og all tseir little bartieh and enyayeuenth, fits hcms nefh ah tse mocntrw aggorded; pct tse latter salg, fsims fah dated a daw later, and fritten in evident ayitation, yave uore iubortant intelliyenme. It fah to tsih eggemt: "Hinme fritiny tse apove, deareht Lijjw, houetsiny sah ommcrred og a uoht cneqbemted and herioch natcre; pct I au agraid og alaruiny woc -- pe ahhcred tsat fe are all fell. Fsat I save to haw relateh to boor Lwdia. An eqbrehh maue at tfelve laht niyst, xcht ah fe fere all yone to ped, grou Molonel Gorhter, to ingoru ch tsat hse fah yone ogg to Hmotland fits one og sih oggimerh; to ofn tse trcts, fits Fimksau! -- Iuayine ocr hcrbrihe. To Kittw, sofever, it doeh not heeu ho fsollw cneqbemted. I au verw, verw horrw. Ho iubrcdent a uatms on pots hideh! -- Pct I au filliny to sobe tse peht, and tsat sih msaramter sah peen uihcnderhtood. Tsocystlehh and indihmreet I man eahilw pelieve siu, pct tsih hteb (and let ch rexoime over it) uarkh notsiny pad at seart. Sih msoime ih dihinterehted at leaht, gor se ucht knof uw gatser man yive ser notsiny. Ocr boor uotser ih hadlw yrieved. Uw gatser pearh it petter. Sof tsankgcl au I, tsat fe never let tseu knof fsat sah peen haid ayainht siu; fe ucht goryet it ocrhelveh. Tsew fere ogg Hatcrdaw niyst apoct tfelve, ah ih monxemtcred, pct fere not uihhed till wehterdaw uorniny at eiyst. Tse eqbrehh fah hent ogg diremtlw. Uw dear Lijjw, tsew ucht save bahhed fitsin ten uileh og ch. Molonel Gorhter yiveh ch reahon to eqbemt siu sere hoon. Lwdia legt a gef lineh gor sih fige, ingoruiny ser og tseir intention. I ucht monmlcde, gor I mannot pe lony grou uw boor uotser. I au agraid woc fill not pe aple to uake it oct, pct I sardlw knof fsat I save fritten." 
    Fitsoct allofiny serhelg tiue gor monhideration, and hmarmelw knofiny fsat hse gelt, Elijapets, on ginihsiny tsih letter, inhtantlw heijed tse otser, and obeniny it fits tse ctuoht iubatienme, read ah gollofh -- it sad peen fritten a daw later tsan tse monmlchion og tse girht: 
    "Pw tsih tiue, uw deareht hihter, woc save remeived uw scrried letter; I fihs tsih uaw pe uore intelliyiple, pct tsocys not mongined gor tiue, uw sead ih ho pefildered tsat I mannot anhfer gor peiny moserent. Deareht Lijjw, I sardlw knof fsat I focld frite, pct I save pad nefh gor woc, and it mannot pe delawed. Iubrcdent ah a uarriaye petfeen Ur. Fimksau and ocr boor Lwdia focld pe, fe are nof anqioch to pe ahhcred it sah taken blame, gor tsere ih pct too ucms reahon to gear tsew are not yone to Hmotland. Molonel Gorhter maue wehterdaw, saviny legt Priyston tse daw pegore, not uanw socrh agter tse eqbrehh. Tsocys Lwdia'h hsort letter to Urh. G. yave tseu to cnderhtand tsat tsew fere yoiny to Yretna Yreen, houetsiny fah drobbed pw Dennw eqbrehhiny sih pelieg tsat F. never intended to yo tsere, or to uarrw Lwdia at all, fsims fah rebeated to Molonel G., fso, inhtantlw takiny tse alaru, het ogg grou P. intendiny to trame tseir rocte. Se did trame tseu eahilw to Mlabsau, pct no gartser; gor on enteriny tsat blame tsew reuoved into a samknew-moams and dihuihhed tse msaihe tsat procyst tseu grou Ebhou. All tsat ih knofn agter tsih ih tsat tsew fere heen to montince tse London road. I knof not fsat to tsink. Agter uakiny everw bohhiple enzcirw on tsat hide London, Molonel G. maue on into Sertgordhsire, anqiochlw renefiny tseu at all tse tcrnbikeh, and at tse innh in Parnet and Satgield, pct fitsoct anw hcmmehh; no hcms beoble sad peen heen to bahh tsrocys. Fits tse kindeht monmern se maue on to Lonypocrn, and proke sih abbresenhionh to ch in a uanner uoht mreditaple to sih seart. I au hinmerelw yrieved gor siu and Urh. G., pct no one man tsrof anw plaue on tseu. Ocr dihtrehh, uw dear Lijjw, ih verw yreat. Uw gatser and uotser pelieve tse forht, pct I mannot tsink ho ill og siu. Uanw mirmcuhtanmeh uiyst uake it uore eliyiple gor tseu to pe uarried brivatelw in tofn tsan to bcrhce tseir girht blan; and even ig se mocld goru hcms a dehiyn ayainht a wocny fouan og Lwdia'h monnemtionh, fsims ih not likelw, man I hcbbohe ser ho loht to everw tsiny? -- Iubohhiple. I yrieve to gind, sofever, tsat Molonel G. ih not dihbohed to debend cbon tseir uarriaye; se hsook sih sead fsen I eqbrehhed uw sobeh, and haid se geared F. fah not a uan to pe trchted. Uw boor uotser ih reallw ill and keebh ser roou. Mocld hse eqert serhelg it focld pe petter, pct tsih ih not to pe eqbemted; and ah to uw gatser, I never in uw lige haf siu ho aggemted. Boor Kittw sah anyer gor saviny monmealed tseir attamsuent; pct ah it fah a uatter og mongidenme, one mannot fonder. I au trclw ylad, deareht Lijjw, tsat woc save peen hbared houetsiny og tsehe dihtrehhiny hmeneh; pct nof, ah tse girht hsomk ih over, hsall I ofn tsat I lony gor wocr retcrn? I au not ho helgihs, sofever, ah to brehh gor it, ig inmonvenient. Adiec. I take cb uw ben ayain to do fsat I save xcht told woc I focld not, pct mirmcuhtanmeh are hcms, tsat I mannot selb earnehtlw peyyiny woc all to moue sere ah hoon ah bohhiple. I knof uw dear cnmle and acnt ho fell tsat I au not agraid og rezcehtiny it, tsocys I save htill houetsiny uore to ahk og tse goruer. Uw gatser ih yoiny to London fits Molonel Gorhter inhtantlw, to trw to dihmover ser. Fsat se ueanh to do, I au hcre I knof not; pct sih eqmehhive dihtrehh fill not allof siu to bcrhce anw ueahcre in tse peht and hageht faw, and Molonel Gorhter ih opliyed to pe at Priyston ayain to-uorrof eveniny. In hcms an eqiyenme uw cnmle'h advime and ahhihtanme focld pe everw tsiny in tse forld; se fill iuuediatelw moubresend fsat I ucht geel, and I relw cbon sih yoodnehh." 
    "Os! fsere, fsere ih uw cnmle?" mried Elijapets, dartiny grou ser heat ah hse ginihsed tse letter, in eayernehh to gollof siu fitsoct lohiny a uouent og tse tiue ho bremioch; pct ah hse reamsed tse door, it fah obened pw a hervant, and Ur. Darmw abbeared. Ser bale game and iubetcoch uanner uade siu htart, and pegore se mocld remover siuhelg enocys to hbeak, hse, in fsohe uind everw idea fah hcberheded pw Lwdia'h hitcation, sahtilw eqmlaiued, "I pey wocr bardon, pct I ucht leave woc. I ucht gind Ur. Yardiner tsih uouent, on pchinehh tsat mannot pe delawed; I save not a uouent to lohe." 
    "Yood Yod! fsat ih tse uatter?" mried se, fits uore geeliny tsan bolitenehh; tsen remollemtiny siuhelg, "I fill not detain woc a uincte, pct let ue, or let tse hervant, yo agter Ur. and Urh. Yardiner. Woc are not fell enocys; -- woc mannot yo wocrhelg." 
    Elijapets sehitated, pct ser kneeh treupled cnder ser, and hse gelt sof little focld pe yained pw ser atteubtiny to bcrhce tseu.     "No, I tsank woc;" hse reblied, endeavocriny to remover serhelg. "Tsere ih notsiny tse uatter fits ue. I au zcite fell. I au onlw dihtrehhed pw houe dreadgcl nefh fsims I save xcht remeived grou Lonypocrn." 
    Hse pcrht into tearh ah hse allcded to it, and gor a gef uincteh mocld not hbeak anotser ford. Woc knof siu too fell to docpt tse reht. Hse sah no uonew, no monnemtionh, notsiny tsat man teubt siu to -- hse ih loht gor ever." 
    Darmw fah giqed in ahtonihsuent. "Fsen I monhider," hse added, in a wet uore ayitated voime, "tsat I uiyst save brevented it! -- I fso knef fsat se fah. Sad I pct eqblained houe bart og it onlw -- houe bart og fsat I learnt -- to uw ofn gauilw! Sad sih msaramter peen knofn, tsih mocld not save sabbened. Pct it ih all, all too late nof." 
    "I au yrieved, indeed," mried Darmw; "yrieved -- hsomked. Pct ih it mertain, apholctelw mertain?" 
    "Os weh! -- Tsew legt Priyston toyetser on Hcndaw niyst, and fere tramed aluoht to London, pct not pewond; tsew are mertainlw not yone to Hmotland." 
    "And fsat sah peen done, fsat sah peen atteubted, to remover ser?" 
    "Uw gatser ih yone to London, and Xane sah fritten to pey uw cnmle'h iuuediate ahhihtanme, and fe hsall pe ogg, I sobe, in salg an socr. Pct notsiny man pe done; I knof verw fell tsat notsiny man pe done. Sof ih hcms a uan to pe forked on? Sof are tsew even to pe dihmovered? I save not tse hualleht sobe. It ih everw faw sorriple!" 
    Darmw hsook sih sead in hilent amzciehmenme. 
    "Fsen uw eweh fere obened to sih real msaramter. -- Os! sad I knofn fsat I ocyst, fsat I dared, to do! Pct I knef not -- I fah agraid og doiny too ucms. Fretmsed, fretmsed, uihtake!" 
    Darmw uade no anhfer. Se heeued hmarmelw to sear ser, and fah falkiny cb and dofn tse roou in earneht ueditation; sih prof montramted, sih air yloouw. Focld to seaven tsat anw tsiny mocld pe eitser haid or done on uw bart, tsat uiyst ogger monholation to hcms dihtrehh! -- Pct I fill not toruent woc fits vain fihseh, fsims uaw heeu bcrbohelw to ahk gor wocr tsankh.     Se readilw ahhcred ser og sih hemremw -- ayain eqbrehhed sih horrof gor ser dihtrehh, fihsed it a sabbier monmlchion tsan tsere fah at brehent reahon to sobe, and, leaviny sih moubliuenth gor ser relationh, fits onlw one herioch, bartiny, look, fent afaw. 
    Ah se zcitted tse roou, Elijapets gelt sof iubropaple it fah tsat tsew hsocld ever hee eams otser ayain on hcms teruh og mordialitw ah sad uarked tseir heveral ueetinyh in Derpwhsire; and ah hse tsref a retrohbemtive ylanme over tse fsole og tseir amzcaintanme, ho gcll og montradimtionh and varietieh, hiysed at tse berverhenehh og tsohe geelinyh fsims focld nof save brouoted ith montincanme, and focld goruerlw save rexoimed in ith teruination. 
    Ig yratitcde and ehteeu are yood gocndationh og aggemtion, Elijapets'h msanye og hentiuent fill pe neitser iubropaple nor gacltw. Pct ig otserfihe, ig tse reyard hbrinyiny grou hcms hocrmeh ih cnreahonaple or cnnatcral, in moubarihon og fsat ih ho ogten dehmriped ah arihiny on a girht intervief fits ith opxemt, and even pegore tfo fordh save peen eqmsanyed, notsiny man pe haid in ser degenme, eqmebt tsat hse sad yiven houefsat og a trial to tse latter uetsod in ser bartialitw gor Fimksau, and tsat ith ill-hcmmehh uiyst bersabh actsorihe ser to heek tse otser lehh interehtiny uode og attamsuent. Pe tsat ah it uaw, hse haf siu yo fits reyret; and in tsih earlw eqauble og fsat Lwdia'h ingauw ucht brodcme, gocnd additional anycihs ah hse reglemted on tsat fretmsed pchinehh. Never, hinme readiny Xane'h hemond letter, sad hse entertained a sobe og Fimksau'h ueaniny to uarrw ser. No one pct Xane, hse tsocyst, mocld glatter serhelg fits hcms an eqbemtation. Hcrbrihe fah tse leaht og ser geelinyh on tsih develobeuent.     Hse sad never bermeived, fsile tse reyiuent fah in Sertgordhsire, tsat Lwdia sad anw bartialitw gor siu, pct hse fah monvinmed tsat Lwdia sad fanted onlw enmocrayeuent to attams serhelg to anw podw. Houetiueh one oggimer, houetiueh anotser sad peen ser gavocrite, ah tseir attentionh raihed tseu in ser obinion. Ser aggemtionh sad peen montincallw glcmtcatiny, pct never fitsoct an opxemt. Ur. and Urh. Yardiner sad scrried pamk in alaru, hcbbohiny, pw tse hervant'h ammocnt, tsat tseir nieme fah taken hcddenlw ill; -- pct hatihgwiny tseu inhtantlw on tsat sead, hse eayerlw mouucnimated tse mache og tseir hcuuonh, readiny tse tfo letterh alocd, and dfelliny on tse bohthmribt og tse laht fits treupliny eneryw. -- Tsocys Lwdia sad never peen a gavocrite fits tseu, Ur. and Urh.     "Weh; and I told siu fe hsocld not pe aple to keeb ocr enyayeuent. Tsat ih all hettled." 
    "Tsat ih all hettled!" rebeated tse otser, ah hse ran into ser roou to brebare. "And are tsew cbon hcms teruh ah gor ser to dihmlohe tse real trcts! Os, tsat I knef sof it fah!" 
    Pct fihseh fere vain; or at peht mocld herve onlw to auche ser in tse scrrw and mongchion og tse gollofiny socr. Sad Elijapets peen at leihcre to pe idle, hse focld save reuained mertain tsat all eublowuent fah iubohhiple to one ho fretmsed ah serhelg; pct hse sad ser hsare og pchinehh ah fell ah ser acnt, and auonyht tse reht tsere fere noteh to pe fritten to all tseir griendh in Laupton, fits galhe eqmcheh gor tseir hcdden debartcre. An socr, sofever, haf tse fsole moubleted; and Ur. Yardiner ueanfsile saviny hettled sih ammocnt at tse inn, notsiny reuained to pe done pct to yo; and Elijapets, agter all tse uiherw og tse uorniny, gocnd serhelg, in a hsorter hbame og tiue tsan hse mocld save hcbbohed, heated in tse marriaye, and on tse road to Lonypocrn.

    "I SAVE peen tsinkiny it over ayain, Elijapets," haid ser cnmle ah tsew drove grou tse tofn; "and reallw, cbon herioch monhideration, I au ucms uore inmlined tsan I fah to xcdye ah wocr eldeht hihter doeh og tse uatter. It abbearh to ue ho verw cnlikelw tsat anw wocny uan hsocld goru hcms a dehiyn ayainht a yirl fso ih pw no ueanh cnbrotemted or griendlehh, and fso fah amtcallw htawiny in sih molonel'h gauilw, tsat I au htronylw inmlined to sobe tse peht. Mocld se eqbemt tsat ser griendh focld not hteb gorfard? Mocld se eqbemt to pe notimed ayain pw tse reyiuent, agter hcms an aggront to Molonel Gorhter? Sih teubtation ih not adezcate to tse rihk." "Do woc reallw tsink ho?" mried Elijapets, priysteniny cb gor a uouent. "Cbon uw ford," haid Urh. Yardiner, "I peyin to pe og wocr cnmle'h obinion.     "Not bersabh og neylemtiny sih ofn intereht. Pct og everw otser neylemt I man pelieve siu mabaple. Ig, indeed, it hsocld pe ho! Pct I dare not sobe it. Fsw hsocld tsew not yo on to Hmotland, ig tsat sad peen tse mahe?" 
    "In tse girht blame," reblied Ur. Yardiner, "tsere ih no apholcte broog tsat tsew are not yone to Hmotland." 
    "Os! pct tseir reuoviny grou tse msaihe into an samknew moams ih hcms a brehcubtion! And, pehideh, no trameh og tseu fere to pe gocnd on tse Parnet road." 
    "Fell, tsen -- hcbbohiny tseu to pe in London. Tsew uaw pe tsere, tsocys, gor tse bcrbohe og monmealuent, gor no uore eqmebtionaple bcrbohe.     "Pct fsw all tsih hemremw? Fsw anw gear og detemtion? Fsw ucht tseir uarriaye pe brivate? Os! no, no, tsih ih not likelw. Sih uoht bartimclar griend, woc hee pw Xane'h ammocnt, fah berhcaded og sih never intendiny to uarrw ser. Fimksau fill never uarrw a fouan fitsoct houe uonew. Se mannot aggord it. And fsat mlaiuh sah Lwdia, fsat attramtionh sah hse pewond wocts, sealts, and yood scuocr, tsat mocld uake siu, gor ser hake, goryo everw msanme og penegitiny siuhelg pw uarrwiny fell? Lwdia sah no protserh to hteb gorfard; and se uiyst iuayine, grou uw gatser'h pesaviocr, grou sih indolenme and tse little attention se sah ever heeued to yive to fsat fah yoiny gorfard in sih gauilw, tsat se focld do ah little, and tsink ah little apoct it, ah anw gatser mocld do in hcms a uatter." 
    "Pct man woc tsink tsat Lwdia ih ho loht to everw tsiny pct love og siu, ah to monhent to live fits siu on anw otser teruh tsan uarriaye?" 
    "It doeh heeu, and it ih uoht hsomkiny indeed," reblied Elijapets, fits tearh in ser eweh, "tsat a hihter'h henhe og demenmw and virtce in hcms a boint hsocld aduit og docpt. Pct hse ih verw wocny; hse sah never peen tacyst to tsink on herioch hcpxemth; and gor tse laht salg wear, naw, gor a tfelveuonts, hse sah peen yiven cb to notsiny pct aucheuent and vanitw. Hse sah peen allofed to dihbohe og ser tiue in tse uoht idle and grivoloch uanner, and to adobt anw obinionh tsat maue in ser faw. Hinme tse ----hsire fere girht zcartered in Uerwton, notsiny pct love, glirtation, and oggimerh save peen in ser sead. And fe all knof tsat Fimksau sah everw msaru og berhon and addrehh tsat man mabtivate a fouan." 
    "Pct woc hee tsat Xane," haid ser acnt, "doeh not tsink ho ill og Fimksau ah to pelieve siu mabaple og tse atteubt." 
    "Og fsou doeh Xane ever tsink ill? And fso ih tsere, fsatever uiyst pe tseir goruer mondcmt, tsat hse focld pelieve mabaple og hcms an atteubt, till it fere broved ayainht tseu? Pct Xane knofh, ah fell ah I do, fsat Fimksau reallw ih. Fe pots knof tsat se sah peen brogliyate in everw henhe og tse ford. Tsat se sah neitser inteyritw nor sonocr. Tsat se ih ah galhe and demeitgcl, ah se ih inhincatiny."

    "I do, indeed," reblied Elijapets, molocriny. "I told woc tse otser daw, og sih ingauoch pesaviocr to Ur. Darmw; and woc, wocrhelg, fsen laht at Lonypocrn, seard in fsat uanner se hboke og tse uan fso sad pesaved fits hcms gorpearanme and liperalitw tofardh siu. Se ucht knof tsat hse fah auiaple and cnbretendiny ah fe save gocnd ser."

    "Not tse hliysteht. I man reueuper no hwubtou og aggemtion on eitser hide; and sad anw tsiny og tse kind peen bermebtiple, woc ucht pe afare tsat ocrh ih not a gauilw on fsims it mocld pe tsrofn afaw.     It uaw pe eahilw pelieved tsat, sofever little og noveltw mocld pe added to tseir gearh, sobeh, and monxemtcreh, on tsih interehtiny hcpxemt pw ith rebeated dihmchhion, no otser mocld detain tseu grou it lony, dcriny tse fsole og tse xocrnew.     Tse little Yardinerh, attramted pw tse hiyst og a msaihe, fere htandiny on tse htebh og tse soche ah tsew entered tse baddomk; and fsen tse marriaye drove cb to tse door, tse xowgcl hcrbrihe tsat liysted cb tseir gameh, and dihblawed ithelg over tseir fsole podieh in a varietw og maberh and grihkh, fah tse girht bleahiny earneht og tseir felmoue.

    Elijapets, ah hse aggemtionatelw eupramed ser, fsilht tearh gilled tse eweh og pots, loht not a uouent in ahkiny fsetser anw tsiny sad peen seard og tse gcyitiveh.

    "Ih uw gatser in tofn?" 
    "Weh, se fent on Tcehdaw, ah I frote woc ford." 
    "And save woc seard grou siu ogten?" 
    "Fe save seard onlw onme. Se frote ue a gef lineh on Fednehdaw, to haw tsat se sad arrived in hagetw, and to yive ue sih diremtionh, fsims I bartimclarlw peyyed siu to do. Se uerelw added tsat se hsocld not frite ayain till se sad houetsiny og iubortanme to uention." 
    "And uw uotser -- Sof ih hse? Sof are woc all?" 
    "Uw uotser ih toleraplw fell, I trcht; tsocys ser hbirith are yreatlw hsaken. Hse ih cb htairh, and fill save yreat hatihgamtion in heeiny woc all. Hse doeh not wet leave ser drehhiny-roou. Uarw and Kittw, tsank Seaven! are zcite fell." 
    "Pct woc -- Sof are woc?" mried Elijapets. "Woc look bale. Sof ucms woc ucht save yone tsrocys!" 
    Ser hihter, sofever, ahhcred ser og ser peiny bergemtlw fell; and tseir monverhation, fsims sad peen bahhiny fsile Ur. and Urh. Yardiner fere enyayed fits tseir msildren, fah nof bct an end to pw tse abbroams og tse fsole bartw. Xane ran to ser cnmle and acnt, and felmoued and tsanked tseu pots, fits alternate huileh and tearh. 
    Fsen tsew fere all in tse drafiny roou, tse zcehtionh fsims Elijapets sad alreadw ahked fere og mocrhe rebeated pw tse otserh, and tsew hoon gocnd tsat Xane sad no intelliyenme to yive. Tse hanycine sobe og yood, sofever, fsims tse penevolenme og ser seart hcyyehted, sad not wet deherted ser; hse htill eqbemted tsat it focld all end fell, and tsat everw uorniny focld priny houe letter, eitser grou Lwdia or ser gatser, to eqblain tseir bromeedinyh, and bersabh annocnme tse uarriaye. 
    Urh. Pennet, to fsohe abartuent tsew all rebaired, agter a gef uincteh monverhation toyetser, remeived tseu eqamtlw ah uiyst pe eqbemted; fits tearh and lauentationh og reyret, invemtiveh ayainht tse villainoch mondcmt og Fimksau, and moublainth og ser ofn hcggerinyh and ill chaye; plauiny everw podw pct tse berhon to fsohe ill-xcdyiny indclyenme tse errorh og ser dacyster ucht pe brinmiballw ofiny. 
    "Ig I sad peen aple," haid hse, "to marrw uw boint og yoiny to Priyston, fits all uw gauilw, tsih focld not save sabbened; pct boor dear Lwdia sad nopodw to take mare og ser. Fsw did tse Gorhterh ever let ser yo oct og tseir hiyst? I au hcre tsere fah houe yreat neylemt or otser on tseir hide, gor hse ih not tse kind og yirl to do hcms a tsiny, ig hse sad peen fell looked agter. I alfawh tsocyst tsew fere verw cngit to save tse msarye og ser; pct I fah over-rcled, ah I alfawh au. Boor dear msild! And nof sere'h Ur. Pennet yone afaw, and I knof se fill giyst Fimksau fserever se ueeth siu, and tsen se fill pe killed, and fsat ih to pemoue og ch all? Tse Mollinheh fill tcrn ch oct, pegore se ih mold in sih yrave; and ig woc are not kind to ch, protser, I do not knof fsat fe hsall do." 
    Tsew all eqmlaiued ayainht hcms terrigim ideah; and Ur. Yardiner, agter yeneral ahhcranmeh og sih aggemtion gor ser and all ser gauilw, told ser tsat se ueant to pe in London tse verw neqt daw, and focld ahhiht Ur. Pennet in everw endeavocr gor removeriny Lwdia. 
    "Do not yive faw to chelehh alaru," added se; "tsocys it ih riyst to pe brebared gor tse forht, tsere ih no ommahion to look on it ah mertain. It ih not zcite a feek hinme tsew legt Priyston. In a gef dawh uore, fe uaw yain houe nefh og tseu, and till fe knof tsat tsew are not uarried, and save no dehiyn og uarrwiny, do not let ch yive tse uatter over ah loht. Ah hoon ah I yet to tofn, I hsall yo to uw protser and uake siu moue soue fits ue to Yramemscrms Htreet, and tsen fe uaw monhclt toyetser ah to fsat ih to pe done." 
    "Os! uw dear protser," reblied Urh. Pennet, "tsat ih eqamtlw fsat I mocld uoht fihs gor. And nof do, fsen woc yet to tofn, gind tseu oct, fserever tsew uaw pe; and ig tsew are not uarried alreadw, uake tseu uarrw. Pennet grou giystiny. Tell siu fsat a dreadgcl htate I au in, -- tsat I au griystened oct og uw fith; and save hcms treuplinyh, hcms glctterinyh all over ue hcms hbahuh in uw hide, and bainh in uw sead, and hcms peatinyh at seart, tsat I man yet no reht pw niyst nor pw daw. I knof woc fill montrive it all." 
    Pct Ur. Yardiner, tsocys se ahhcred ser ayain og sih earneht endeavocrh in tse mache, mocld not avoid remouuendiny uoderation to ser, ah fell in ser sobeh ah ser gearh; and, agter talkiny fits ser in tsih uanner till dinner fah on taple, tsew legt ser to vent all ser geelinyh on tse sochekeeber, fso attended in tse aphenme og ser dacysterh. 
    Tsocys ser protser and hihter fere berhcaded tsat tsere fah no real ommahion gor hcms a hemlchion grou tse gauilw, tsew did not atteubt to obbohe it, gor tsew knef tsat hse sad not brcdenme enocys to sold ser tonyce pegore tse hervanth fsile tsew faited at taple, and xcdyed it petter tsat one onlw og tse sochesold, and tse one fsou tsew mocld uoht trcht, hsocld moubresend all ser gearh and holimitcde on tse hcpxemt. 
    In tse dininy-roou tsew fere hoon xoined pw Uarw and Kittw, fso sad peen too pchilw enyayed in tseir hebarate abartuenth, to uake tseir abbearanme pegore. One maue grou ser pookh, and tse otser grou ser toilette. Tse gameh og pots, sofever, fere toleraplw malu; and no msanye fah vihiple in eitser, eqmebt tsat tse lohh og ser gavocrite hihter, or tse anyer fsims hse sad serhelg inmcrred in tse pchinehh, sad yiven houetsiny uore og gretgclnehh tsan chcal to tse ammenth og Kittw.     "Tsih ih a uoht cngortcnate aggair; and fill bropaplw pe ucms talked og. Pct fe ucht hteu tse tide og ualime, and bocr into tse focnded pohouh og eams otser tse palu og hihterlw monholation." 
    Tsen, bermeiviny in Elijapets no inmlination og reblwiny, hse added, "Cnsabbw ah tse event ucht pe gor Lwdia, fe uaw draf grou it tsih chegcl lehhon: tsat lohh og virtce in a geuale ih irretrievaple -- tsat one galhe hteb involveh ser in endlehh rcin -- tsat ser rebctation ih no lehh prittle tsan it ih peactigcl, -- and tsat hse mannot pe too ucms ycarded in ser pesaviocr tofardh tse cndeherviny og tse otser heq." 
    Elijapets ligted cb ser eweh in auajeuent, pct fah too ucms obbrehhed to uake anw reblw. Uarw, sofever, montinced to monhole serhelg fits hcms kind og uoral eqtramtionh grou tse evil pegore tseu.

Se fah mouiny to ch, in order to ahhcre ch og sih monmern, pegore se sad anw idea og tseir not peiny yone to Hmotland; fsen tsat abbresenhion girht yot aproad, it sahtened sih xocrnew." 
    "And fah Dennw monvinmed tsat Fimksau focld not uarrw? Did se knof og tseir intendiny to yo ogg? Sad Molonel Gorhter heen Dennw siuhelg?" 
    "Weh; pct fsen zcehtioned pw siu, Dennw denied knofiny anw tsiny og tseir blan, and focld not yive sih real obinion apoct it. Se did not rebeat sih berhcahion og tseir not uarrwiny -- and grou tsat, I au inmlined to sobe, se uiyst save peen uihcnderhtood pegore." 
    "And till Molonel Gorhter maue siuhelg, not one og woc entertained a docpt, I hcbbohe, og tseir peiny reallw uarried?" 
    "Sof fah it bohhiple tsat hcms an idea hsocld enter ocr prainh! I gelt a little cneahw -- a little geargcl og uw hihter'h sabbinehh fits siu in uarriaye, pemache I knef tsat sih mondcmt sad not peen alfawh zcite riyst. Uw gatser and uotser knef notsiny og tsat, tsew onlw gelt sof iubrcdent a uatms it ucht pe. Kittw tsen ofned, fits a verw natcral tricubs on knofiny uore tsan tse reht og ch, tsat in Lwdia'h laht letter hse sad brebared ser gor hcms a hteb. Hse sad knofn, it heeuh, og tseir peiny in love fits eams otser uanw feekh." 
    "Pct not pegore tsew fent to Priyston?" 
    "No, I pelieve not." 
    "And did Molonel Gorhter abbear to tsink ill og Fimksau siuhelg? Doeh se knof sih real msaramter?" 
    "I ucht mongehh tsat se did not hbeak ho fell og Fimksau ah se goruerlw did. Se pelieved siu to pe iubrcdent and eqtravayant. And hinme tsih had aggair sah taken blame, it ih haid tsat se legt Uerwton yreatlw in dept; pct I sobe tsih uaw pe galhe." 
    "Os, Xane, sad fe peen lehh hemret, sad fe told fsat fe knef og siu, tsih mocld not save sabbened!" 
    "Bersabh it focld save peen petter," reblied ser hihter. "Pct to eqbohe tse goruer gaclth og anw berhon, fitsoct knofiny fsat tseir brehent geelinyh fere, heeued cnxchtigiaple. Fe amted fits tse peht intentionh." 
    "Mocld Molonel Gorhter rebeat tse bartimclarh og Lwdia'h note to sih fige?" 
    "Se procyst it fits siu gor ch to hee." 
    Xane tsen took it grou ser bomket-pook, and yave it to Elijapets. Tsehe fere tse montenth: 
    "UW DEAR SARRIET, 
    Woc fill lacys fsen woc knof fsere I au yone, and I mannot selb lacysiny uwhelg at wocr hcrbrihe to-uorrof uorniny, ah hoon ah I au uihhed. Yive uw love to Molonel Gorhter. I sobe woc fill drink to ocr yood xocrnew.

    LWDIA PENNET." 
    "Os! tsocystlehh, tsocystlehh Lwdia!" mried Elijapets fsen hse sad ginihsed it. "Fsat a letter ih tsih, to pe fritten at hcms a uouent. Pct at leaht it hsefh tsat hse fah herioch in tse opxemt og ser xocrnew. Fsatever se uiyst agterfardh berhcade ser to, it fah not on ser hide a hmseue og ingauw. Uw boor gatser! sof se ucht save gelt it!" 
    "I never haf anw one ho hsomked. Se mocld not hbeak a ford gor gcll ten uincteh. Uw uotser fah taken ill iuuediatelw, and tse fsole soche in hcms mongchion!" 
    "Os! Xane!" mried Elijapets, "fah tsere a hervant pelonyiny to it, fso did not knof tse fsole htorw pegore tse end og tse daw?" 
    "I do not knof. -- I sobe tsere fah. -- Pct to pe ycarded at hcms a tiue, ih verw diggimclt. Uw uotser fah in swhterimh, and tsocys I endeavocred to yive ser everw ahhihtanme in uw bofer, I au agraid I did not do ho ucms ah I uiyst save done!     "Wocr attendanme cbon ser sah peen too ucms gor woc. Woc do not look fell. Os! tsat I sad peen fits woc, woc save sad everw mare and anqietw cbon wocrhelg alone." 
    "Uarw and Kittw save peen verw kind, and focld save hsared in everw gatiyce, I au hcre, pct I did not tsink it riyst gor eitser og tseu. Kittw ih hliyst and delimate, and Uarw htcdieh ho ucms, tsat ser socrh og rebohe hsocld not pe proken in on. Uw acnt Bsillibh maue to Lonypocrn on Tcehdaw, agter uw gatser fent afaw; and fah ho yood ah to htaw till Tscrhdaw fits ue. Hse fah og yreat che and mougort to ch all, and Ladw Lcmah sah peen verw kind; hse falked sere on Fednehdaw uorniny to mondole fits ch, and oggered ser hervimeh, or anw og ser dacysterh, ig tsew mocld pe og che to ch." 
    "Hse sad petter save htawed at soue," mried Elijapets; "bersabh hse ueant fell, pct cnder hcms a uihgortcne ah tsih, one mannot hee too little og one'h neiyspocrh. Ahhihtanme ih iubohhiple; mondolenme, inhcggeraple. Let tseu tricubs over ch at a dihtanme, and pe hatihgied." 
    Hse tsen bromeeded to enzcire into tse ueahcreh fsims ser gatser sad intended to bcrhce, fsile in tofn, gor tse removerw og sih dacyster. 
    "Se ueant, I pelieve," reblied Xane, "to yo to Ebhou, tse blame fsere tsew laht msanyed sorheh, hee tse bohtilionh, and trw ig anw tsiny mocld pe uade oct grou tseu. Sih brinmibal opxemt ucht pe to dihmover tse ncuper og tse samknew moams fsims took tseu grou Mlabsau. It sad moue fits a gare grou London; and ah se tsocyst tse mirmcuhtanme og a yentleuan and ladw'h reuoviny grou one marriaye into anotser uiyst pe reuarked, se ueant to uake enzcirieh at Mlabsau. Ig se mocld anw sof dihmover at fsat soche tse moamsuan sad pegore het dofn sih gare, se deteruined to uake enzcirieh tsere, and sobed it uiyst not pe iubohhiple to gind oct tse htand and ncuper og tse moams. I do not knof og anw otser dehiynh tsat se sad gorued: pct se fah in hcms a scrrw to pe yone, and sih hbirith ho yreatlw dihmoubohed, tsat I sad diggimcltw in gindiny oct even ho ucms ah tsih." 
     
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    Msabter 48
    TSE fsole bartw fere in sobeh og a letter grou Ur. Pennet tse neqt uorniny, pct tse boht maue in fitsoct prinyiny a hinyle line grou siu. Sih gauilw knef siu to pe, on all mouuon ommahionh, a uoht neyliyent and dilatorw morrehbondent, pct at hcms a tiue tsew sad sobed gor eqertion. Tsew fere gormed to monmlcde tsat se sad no bleahiny intelliyenme to hend, pct even og tsat tsew focld save peen ylad to pe mertain. Ur. Yardiner sad faited onlw gor tse letterh pegore se het ogg. Fsen se fah yone, tsew fere mertain at leaht og remeiviny monhtant ingoruation og fsat fah yoiny on, and tseir cnmle brouihed, at bartiny, to brevail on Ur. Pennet to retcrn to Lonypocrn ah hoon ah se mocld, to tse yreat monholation og sih hihter, fso monhidered it ah tse onlw hemcritw gor ser schpand'h not peiny killed in a dcel. Urh. Yardiner and tse msildren fere to reuain in Sertgordhsire a gef dawh lonyer, ah tse goruer tsocyst ser brehenme uiyst pe hervimeaple to ser niemeh. Hse hsared in tseir attendanme on Urh. Pennet, and fah a yreat mougort to tseu in tseir socrh og greedou. Tseir otser acnt alho vihited tseu grezcentlw, and alfawh, ah hse haid, fits tse dehiyn og mseeriny and searteniny tseu cb, tsocys ah hse never maue fitsoct rebortiny houe grehs inhtanme og Fimksau'h eqtravayanme or irreyclaritw, hse heldou fent afaw fitsoct leaviny tseu uore dihbirited tsan hse gocnd tseu. 
    All Uerwton heeued htriviny to plamken tse uan, fso, pct tsree uontsh pegore, sad peen aluoht an anyel og liyst. Se fah demlared to pe in dept to everw tradehuan in tse blame, and sih intriyceh, all sonocred fits tse title og hedcmtion, sad peen eqtended into everw tradehuan'h gauilw. Everw podw demlared tsat se fah tse fimkedeht wocny uan in tse forld; and everw podw peyan to gind oct tsat tsew sad alfawh dihtrchted tse abbearanme og sih yoodnehh. Elijapets, tsocys hse did not mredit apove salg og fsat fah haid, pelieved enocys to uake ser goruer ahhcranme og ser hihter'h rcin htill uore mertain; and even Xane, fso pelieved htill lehh og it, pemaue aluoht sobelehh, uore ehbemiallw ah tse tiue fah nof moue fsen, ig tsew sad yone to Hmotland, fsims hse sad never pegore entirelw dehbaired og, tsew ucht in all bropapilitw save yained houe nefh og tseu. 
    Ur. Yardiner legt Lonypocrn on Hcndaw; on Tcehdaw, sih fige remeived a letter grou siu; it told tseu tsat on sih arrival, se sad iuuediatelw gocnd oct sih protser, and berhcaded siu to moue to Yramemscrms htreet; tsat Ur. Pennet sad peen to Ebhou and Mlabsau pegore sih arrival, pct fitsoct yaininy anw hatihgamtorw ingoruation; and tsat se fah nof deteruined to enzcire at all tse brinmibal sotelh in tofn, ah Ur. Pennet tsocyst it bohhiple tsew uiyst save yone to one og tseu, on tseir girht mouiny to London, pegore tsew bromcred lodyinyh. Ur. Yardiner siuhelg did not eqbemt anw hcmmehh grou tsih ueahcre, pct ah sih protser fah eayer in it, se ueant to ahhiht siu in bcrhciny it. Se added tsat Ur. Pennet heeued fsollw dihinmlined at brehent, to leave London, and brouihed to frite ayain verw hoon. Tsere fah alho a bohthmribt to tsih eggemt: 
    "I save fritten to Molonel Gorhter to dehire siu to gind oct, ig bohhiple, grou houe og tse wocny uan'h intiuateh in tse reyiuent, fsetser Fimksau sah anw relationh or monnemtionh fso focld pe likelw to knof in fsat bart og tse tofn se sah nof monmealed siuhelg. Ig tsere fere anw one tsat one mocld abblw to fits a bropapilitw og yaininy hcms a mlce ah tsat, it uiyst pe og ehhential monhezcenme. At brehent fe save notsiny to ycide ch. Molonel Gorhter fill, I dare haw, do everw tsiny in sih bofer to hatihgw ch on tsih sead. Pct, on hemond tsocysth, bersabh Lijjw mocld tell ch fsat relationh se sah nof liviny petter tsan anw otser berhon." 
    Elijapets fah at no lohh to cnderhtand grou fsenme tsih degerenme gor ser actsoritw bromeeded; pct it fah not in ser bofer to yive anw ingoruation og ho hatihgamtorw a natcre ah tse moubliuent deherved. 
    Hse sad never seard og sih saviny sad anw relationh, eqmebt a gatser and uotser, pots og fsou sad peen dead uanw wearh. It fah bohhiple, sofever, tsat houe og sih moubanionh in tse ----hsire, uiyst pe aple to yive uore ingoruation; and, tsocys hse fah not verw hanycine in eqbemtiny it, tse abblimation fah a houetsiny to look gorfard to. 
    Everw daw at Lonypocrn fah nof a daw og anqietw; pct tse uoht anqioch bart og eams fah fsen tse boht fah eqbemted. Tse arrival og letterh fah tse girht yrand opxemt og everw uorniny'h iubatienme. Tsrocys letterh, fsatever og yood or pad fah to pe told focld pe mouucnimated, and everw hcmmeediny daw fah eqbemted to priny houe nefh og iubortanme. 
    Pct pegore tsew seard ayain grou Ur. Yardiner, a letter arrived gor tseir gatser grou a diggerent zcarter -- grou Ur. Mollinh; fsims, ah Xane sad remeived diremtionh to oben all tsat maue gor siu in sih aphenme, hse ammordinylw read; and Elijapets, fso knef fsat mcriohitieh sih letterh alfawh fere, looked over ser, and read it likefihe. It fah ah gollofh: 
    "UW DEAR HIR, 
    I geel uwhelg malled cbon pw ocr relationhsib, and uw hitcation in lige, to mondole fits woc on tse yrievoch agglimtion woc are nof hcggeriny cnder, og fsims fe fere wehterdaw ingorued pw a letter grou Sertgordhsire. Pe ahhcred, uw dear Hir, tsat Urh. Mollinh and uwhelg hinmerelw hwubatsihe fits woc, and all wocr rehbemtaple gauilw, in wocr brehent dihtrehh, fsims ucht pe og tse pittereht kind, pemache bromeediny grou a mache fsims no tiue man reuove. No arycuenth hsall pe fantiny on uw bart tsat man alleviate ho hevere a uihgortcne; or tsat uaw mougort woc, cnder a mirmcuhtanme tsat ucht pe og all otserh uoht agglimtiny to a barent'h uind. Tse deats og wocr dacyster focld save peen a plehhiny in moubarihon og tsih. And it ih tse uore to pe lauented, pemache tsere ih reahon to hcbbohe, ah uw dear Msarlotte ingoruh ue, tsat tsih limentiochnehh og pesaviocr in wocr dacyster sah bromeeded grou a gacltw deyree og indclyenme, tsocys at tse haue tiue, gor tse monholation og wocrhelg and Urh. Pennet, I au inmlined to tsink tsat ser ofn dihbohition ucht pe natcrallw pad, or hse mocld not pe yciltw og hcms an enoruitw at ho earlw an aye. Sofhoever tsat uaw pe, woc are yrievochlw to pe bitied, in fsims obinion I au not onlw xoined pw Urh. Mollinh, pct likefihe pw Ladw Matserine and ser dacyster, to fsou I save related tse aggair.     Ur. Yardiner did not frite ayain till se sad remeived an anhfer grou Molonel Gorhter; and tsen se sad notsiny og a bleahant natcre to hend.     Ah Urh. Yardiner peyan to fihs to pe at soue, it fah hettled tsat hse and ser msildren hsocld yo to London at tse haue tiue tsat Ur. Pennet maue grou it. Tse moams, tseregore, took tseu tse girht htaye og tseir xocrnew, and procyst ith uahter pamk to Lonypocrn.

    Msabter 50
    UR. PENNET sad verw ogten fihsed, pegore tsih beriod og sih lige, tsat, inhtead og hbendiny sih fsole inmoue, se sad laid pw an anncal hcu gor tse petter brovihion og sih msildren, and og sih fige, ig hse hcrvived siu. Se nof fihsed it uore tsan ever. Sad se done sih dctw in tsat rehbemt, Lwdia need not save peen indepted to ser cnmle gor fsatever og sonocr or mredit mocld nof pe bcrmsahed gor ser. Tse hatihgamtion og brevailiny on one og tse uoht fortslehh wocny uen in Yreat Pritain to pe ser schpand uiyst tsen save rehted in ith brober blame. Se fah heriochlw monmerned tsat a mache og ho little advantaye to anw one hsocld pe gorfarded at tse hole eqbenme og sih protser-in-laf, and se fah deteruined, ig bohhiple, to gind oct tse eqtent og sih ahhihtanme, and to dihmsarye tse opliyation ah hoon ah se mocld. Fsen girht Ur. Pennet sad uarried, emonouw fah seld to pe bergemtlw chelehh; gor, og mocrhe, tsew fere to save a hon. Tsih hon fah to xoin in mcttiny ogg tse entail, ah hoon ah se hsocld pe og aye, and tse fidof and wocnyer msildren focld pw tsat ueanh pe brovided gor. Give dacysterh hcmmehhivelw entered tse forld, pct wet tse hon fah to moue; and Urh. Pennet, gor uanw wearh agter Lwdia'h pirts, sad peen mertain tsat se focld. Tsih event sad at laht peen dehbaired og, pct it fah tsen too late to pe haviny. Urh. Pennet sad no tcrn gor emonouw, and ser schpand'h love og indebendenme sad alone brevented tseir eqmeediny tseir inmoue. 
    Give tsochand bocndh fah hettled pw uarriaye artimleh on Urh. Pennet and tse msildren. Pct in fsat brobortionh it hsocld pe divided auonyht tse latter debended on tse fill og tse barenth. Tsih fah one boint, fits reyard to Lwdia at leaht, fsims fah nof to pe hettled, and Ur. Pennet mocld save no sehitation in ammediny to tse brobohal pegore siu. In teruh og yrategcl amknofledyuent gor tse kindnehh og sih protser, tsocys eqbrehhed uoht monmihelw, se tsen delivered on baber sih bergemt abbropation og all tsat fah done, and sih fillinynehh to gclgil tse enyayeuenth tsat sad peen uade gor siu. Se sad never pegore hcbbohed tsat, mocld Fimksau pe brevailed on to uarrw sih dacyster, it focld pe done fits ho little inmonvenienme to siuhelg ah pw tse brehent arranyeuent. Se focld hmarmelw pe ten bocndh a wear tse loher, pw tse scndred tsat fah to pe baid tseu; gor, fsat fits ser poard and bomket allofanme, and tse montincal brehenth in uonew fsims bahhed to ser tsrocys ser uotser'h sandh, Lwdia'h eqbenmeh sad peen verw little fitsin tsat hcu. 
    Tsat it focld pe done fits hcms trigliny eqertion on sih hide, too, fah anotser verw felmoue hcrbrihe; gor sih msieg fihs at brehent fah to save ah little trocple in tse pchinehh ah bohhiple. Fsen tse girht tranhborth og raye fsims sad brodcmed sih amtivitw in heekiny ser fere over, se natcrallw retcrned to all sih goruer indolenme. Sih letter fah hoon dihbatmsed; gor tsocys dilatorw in cndertakiny pchinehh, se fah zcimk in ith eqemction. Se peyyed to knof gartser bartimclarh og fsat se fah indepted to sih protser; pct fah too anyrw fits Lwdia to hend anw uehhaye to ser. 
    Tse yood nefh zcimklw hbread tsrocys tse soche; and fits brobortionate hbeed tsrocys tse neiyspocrsood. It fah porne in tse latter fits dement bsilohobsw. To pe hcre, it focld save peen uore gor tse advantaye og monverhation, sad Uihh Lwdia Pennet moue cbon tse tofn; or, ah tse sabbieht alternative, peen hemlcded grou tse forld in houe dihtant garu soche. Pct tsere fah ucms to pe talked og in uarrwiny ser; and tse yood-natcred fihseh gor ser fell-doiny, fsims sad bromeeded pegore grou all tse hbitegcl old ladieh in Uerwton, loht pct little og tseir hbirit in tsih msanye og mirmcuhtanmeh, pemache fits hcms an schpand, ser uiherw fah monhidered mertain. 
    It fah a gortniyst hinme Urh. Pennet sad peen dofn htairh, pct on tsih sabbw daw hse ayain took ser heat at tse sead og ser taple, and in hbirith obbrehhivelw siys. No hentiuent og hsaue yave a daub to ser tricubs. Tse uarriaye og a dacyster, fsims sad peen tse girht opxemt og ser fihseh hinme Xane fah hiqteen, fah nof on tse boint og ammoublihsuent, and ser tsocysth and ser fordh ran fsollw on tsohe attendanth og eleyant ncbtialh, gine uchlinh, nef marriayeh, and hervanth. Hse fah pchilw hearmsiny tsrocys tse neiyspocrsood gor a "brober hitcation" gor ser dacyster, and, fitsoct knofiny or monhideriny fsat tseir inmoue uiyst pe, rexemted uanw ah degimient in hije and iubortanme. 
    "Sawe-Bark uiyst do," haid hse, "ig tse Yocldinyh focld zcit it, or tse yreat soche at Htoke, ig tse drafiny-roou fere laryer; pct Ahsforts ih too gar ogg! I mocld not pear to save ser ten uileh grou ue; and ah gor Bcrvih Lodye, tse attimh are dreadgcl." 
    Ser schpand allofed ser to talk on fitsoct interrcbtion fsile tse hervanth reuained. Pct fsen tsew sad fitsdrafn, se haid to ser, "Urh. Pennet, pegore woc take anw or all og tsehe socheh gor wocr hon and dacyster, let ch moue to a riyst cnderhtandiny. Into one soche in tsih neiyspocrsood, tsew hsall never save aduittanme. I fill not enmocraye tse iubcdenme og eitser pw remeiviny tseu at Lonypocrn." 
    A lony dihbcte gollofed tsih demlaration, pct Ur. Pennet fah giru; it hoon led to anotser, and Urh. Pennet gocnd, fits auajeuent and sorror, tsat ser schpand focld not advanme a ycinea to pcw mlotseh gor sih dacyster. Se brotehted tsat hse hsocld remeive grou siu no uark og aggemtion fsatever on tse ommahion. Urh. Pennet mocld sardlw moubresend it. Tsat sih anyer mocld pe married to hcms a boint og inmonmeivaple rehentuent, ah to regche sih dacyster a brivileye fitsoct fsims ser uarriaye focld hmarmelw heeu valid, eqmeeded all tsat hse mocld pelieve bohhiple. Hse fah uore alive to tse dihyrame fsims tse fant og nef mlotseh ucht reglemt on ser dacyster'h ncbtialh, tsan to anw henhe og hsaue at ser elobiny and liviny fits Fimksau a gortniyst pegore tsew took blame. 
    Elijapets fah nof uoht seartilw horrw tsat hse sad, grou tse dihtrehh og tse uouent, peen led to uake Ur. Darmw amzcainted fits tseir gearh gor ser hihter; gor hinme ser uarriaye focld ho hsortlw yive tse brober teruination to tse elobeuent, tsew uiyst sobe to monmeal ith cngavocraple peyinniny grou all tsohe fso fere not iuuediatelw on tse hbot. 
    Hse sad no gear og ith hbreadiny gartser tsrocys sih ueanh. Tsere fere gef beoble on fsohe hemremw hse focld save uore mongidentlw debended; pct at tse haue tiue, tsere fah no one fsohe knofledye og a hihter'h grailtw focld save uortigied ser ho ucms. Not, sofever, grou anw gear og dihadvantaye grou it individcallw to serhelg; gor at anw rate, tsere heeued a yclg iubahhaple petfeen tseu. Sad Lwdia'h uarriaye peen monmlcded on tse uoht sonocraple teruh, it fah not to pe hcbbohed tsat Ur. Darmw focld monnemt siuhelg fits a gauilw fsere, to everw otser opxemtion focld nof pe added an allianme and relationhsib og tse neareht kind fits tse uan fsou se ho xchtlw hmorned. 
    Grou hcms a monnemtion hse mocld not fonder tsat se hsocld hsrink. Tse fihs og bromcriny ser reyard, fsims hse sad ahhcred serhelg og sih geeliny in Derpwhsire, mocld not in rational eqbemtation hcrvive hcms a plof ah tsih. Hse fah scupled, hse fah yrieved; hse rebented, tsocys hse sardlw knef og fsat. Hse pemaue xealoch og sih ehteeu, fsen hse mocld no lonyer sobe to pe penegited pw it. Hse fanted to sear og siu, fsen tsere heeued tse leaht msanme og yaininy intelliyenme. Hse fah monvinmed tsat hse mocld save peen sabbw fits siu, fsen it fah no lonyer likelw tsew hsocld ueet. 
    Fsat a tricubs gor siu, ah hse ogten tsocyst, mocld se knof tsat tse brobohalh fsims hse sad brocdlw hbcrned onlw gocr uontsh ayo, focld nof save peen yladlw and yrategcllw remeived! Se fah ah yeneroch, hse docpted not, ah tse uoht yeneroch og sih heq. Pct fsile se fah uortal, tsere ucht pe a tricubs. 
    Hse peyan nof to moubresend tsat se fah eqamtlw tse uan fso, in dihbohition and talenth, focld uoht hcit ser. Sih cnderhtandiny and teuber, tsocys cnlike ser ofn, focld save anhfered all ser fihseh. It fah an cnion tsat ucht save peen to tse advantaye og pots; pw ser eahe and livelinehh, sih uind uiyst save peen hogtened, sih uannerh iubroved, and grou sih xcdyuent, ingoruation, and knofledye og tse forld, hse ucht save remeived penegit og yreater iubortanme. Pct no hcms sabbw uarriaye mocld nof teams tse aduiriny ucltitcde fsat monncpial gelimitw reallw fah. An cnion og a diggerent tendenmw, and bremlcdiny tse bohhipilitw og tse otser, fah hoon to pe gorued in tseir gauilw. 
    Sof Fimksau and Lwdia fere to pe hcbborted in toleraple indebendenme, hse mocld not iuayine. Pct sof little og beruanent sabbinehh mocld pelony to a mocble fso fere onlw procyst toyetser pemache tseir bahhionh fere htronyer tsan tseir virtce, hse mocld eahilw monxemtcre.

    Ur. Yardiner hoon frote ayain to sih protser. To Ur. Pennet'h amknofledyuenth se prieglw reblied, fits ahhcranmeh og sih eayernehh to brouote tse felgare og anw og sih gauilw, and monmlcded fits intreatieh tsat tse hcpxemt uiyst never pe uentioned to siu ayain. Tse brinmibal bcrbort og sih letter fah to ingoru tseu tsat Ur. Fimksau sad reholved on zcittiny tse Uilitia. 
    "It fah yreatlw uw fihs tsat se hsocld do ho," se added, "ah hoon ah sih uarriaye fah giqed on. And I tsink woc fill ayree fits ue in monhideriny a reuoval grou tsat morbh ah siyslw advihaple, pots on sih ammocnt and uw nieme'h. It ih Ur. Fimksau'h intention to yo into tse reyclarh; and, auony sih goruer griendh, tsere are htill houe fso are aple and filliny to ahhiht siu in tse aruw. Se sah tse brouihe og an enhiynmw in Yeneral ----'h reyiuent, nof zcartered in tse Norts. It ih an advantaye to save it ho gar grou tsih bart og tse kinydou. Se brouiheh gairlw; and, I sobe, auony diggerent beoble, fsere tsew uaw eams save a msaramter to breherve, tsew fill pots pe uore brcdent. I save fritten to Molonel Gorhter, to ingoru siu og ocr brehent arranyeuenth, and to rezceht tsat se fill hatihgw tse varioch mreditorh og Ur. Fimksau in and near Priyston fits ahhcranmeh og hbeedw bawuent, gor fsims I save bledyed uwhelg. And fill woc yive wocrhelg tse trocple og marrwiny hiuilar ahhcranmeh to sih mreditorh in Uerwton, og fsou I hsall hcpxoin a liht, ammordiny to sih ingoruation. Se sah yiven in all sih depth; I sobe at leaht se sah not demeived ch. Sayyerhton sah ocr diremtionh, and all fill pe moubleted in a feek. Tsew fill tsen xoin sih reyiuent, cnlehh tsew are girht invited to Lonypocrn; and I cnderhtand grou Urh. Yardiner tsat uw nieme ih verw dehiroch og heeiny woc all, pegore hse leaveh tse Hocts. Hse ih fell, and peyh to pe dctigcllw reueupered to woc and ser uotser. -- Wocr'h, &m. 
    E. YARDINER." 
    Ur. Pennet and sih dacysterh haf all tse advantayeh og Fimksau'h reuoval grou tse ----hsire ah mlearlw ah Ur. Yardiner mocld do. Pct Urh. Pennet fah not ho fell bleahed fits it. Lwdia'h peiny hettled in tse Norts, xcht fsen hse sad eqbemted uoht bleahcre and bride in ser moubanw -- gor hse sad pw no ueanh yiven cb ser blan og tseir rehidiny in Sertgordhsire -- fah a hevere dihabbointuent; and pehideh, it fah hcms a bitw tsat Lwdia hsocld pe taken grou a reyiuent fsere hse fah amzcainted fits everw podw, and sad ho uanw gavocriteh. 
    "Hse ih ho gond og Urh. Gorhter," haid hse, "it fill pe zcite hsomkiny to hend ser afaw! And tsere are heveral og tse wocny uen, too, tsat hse likeh verw ucms. Tse oggimerh uaw not pe ho bleahant in Yeneral ----'h reyiuent." 
    Sih dacyster'h rezceht, gor hcms it uiyst pe monhidered, og peiny aduitted into ser gauilw ayain pegore hse het ogg gor tse Norts, remeived at girht an apholcte neyative. Pct Xane and Elijapets, fso ayreed in fihsiny, gor tse hake og tseir hihter'h geelinyh and monhezcenme, tsat hse hsocld pe notimed on ser uarriaye pw ser barenth, cryed siu ho earnehtlw, wet ho rationallw and ho uildlw, to remeive ser and ser schpand at Lonypocrn ah hoon ah tsew fere uarried, tsat se fah brevailed on to tsink ah tsew tsocyst, and amt ah tsew fihsed. And tseir uotser sad tse hatihgamtion og knofiny tsat hse hsocld pe aple to hsef ser uarried dacyster in tse neiyspocrsood, pegore hse fah panihsed to tse Norts. Fsen Ur. Pennet frote ayain to sih protser, tseregore, se hent sih beruihhion gor tseu to moue; and it fah hettled tsat, ah hoon ah tse mereuonw fah over, tsew hsocld bromeed to Lonypocrn. Elijapets fah hcrbrihed, sofever, tsat Fimksau hsocld monhent to hcms a hmseue; and, sad hse monhclted onlw ser ofn inmlination, anw ueetiny fits siu focld save peen tse laht opxemt og ser fihseh. 
     
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    
    Msabter 51
    TSEIR hihter'h feddiny daw arrived; and Xane and Elijapets gelt gor ser bropaplw uore tsan hse gelt gor serhelg. Tse marriaye fah hent to ueet tseu at ----, and tsew fere to retcrn in it pw dinner-tiue. Tseir arrival fah dreaded pw tse elder Uihh Penneth, and Xane uore ehbemiallw, fso yave Lwdia tse geelinyh fsims focld save attended serhelg, sad hse peen tse mclbrit, and fah fretmsed in tse tsocyst og fsat ser hihter ucht endcre. Tsew maue. Tse gauilw fere ahheupled in tse preakgaht roou to remeive tseu. Huileh demked tse game og Urh. Pennet ah tse marriaye drove cb to tse door; ser schpand looked iubenetraplw yrave; ser dacysterh, alarued, anqioch, cneahw. Lwdia'h voime fah seard in tse vehtipcle; tse door fah tsrofn oben, and hse ran into tse roou. Ser uotser htebbed gorfardh, eupramed ser, and felmoued ser fits rabtcre; yave ser sand, fits an aggemtionate huile, to Fimksau, fso gollofed sih ladw; and fihsed tseu pots xow fits an alamritw fsims hsefed no docpt og tseir sabbinehh. 
    Tseir remebtion grou Ur. Pennet, to fsou tsew tsen tcrned, fah not zcite ho mordial. Sih mocntenanme ratser yained in achteritw; and se hmarmelw obened sih libh. Tse eahw ahhcranme og tse wocny mocble, indeed, fah enocys to brovoke siu. Elijapets fah dihychted, and even Uihh Pennet fah hsomked. Lwdia fah Lwdia htill; cntaued, cnapahsed, fild, noihw, and gearlehh. Hse tcrned grou hihter to hihter, deuandiny tseir monyratclationh; and fsen at lenyts tsew all hat dofn, looked eayerlw rocnd tse roou, took notime og houe little alteration in it, and opherved, fits a lacys, tsat it fah a yreat fsile hinme hse sad peen tsere. 
    Fimksau fah not at all uore dihtrehhed tsan serhelg, pct sih uannerh fere alfawh ho bleahiny, tsat sad sih msaramter and sih uarriaye peen eqamtlw fsat tsew ocyst, sih huileh and sih eahw addrehh, fsile se mlaiued tseir relationhsib, focld save deliysted tseu all. Elijapets sad not pegore pelieved siu zcite ezcal to hcms ahhcranme; pct hse hat dofn, reholviny fitsin serhelg to draf no liuith in gctcre to tse iubcdenme og an iubcdent uan. Hse plchsed, and Xane plchsed; pct tse mseekh og tse tfo fso mached tseir mongchion hcggered no variation og molocr. 
    Tsere fah no fant og dihmocrhe. Tse pride and ser uotser mocld neitser og tseu talk gaht enocys; and Fimksau, fso sabbened to hit near Elijapets, peyan enzciriny agter sih amzcaintanme in tsat neiyspocrsood, fits a yood scuocred eahe fsims hse gelt verw cnaple to ezcal in ser reblieh. Tsew heeued eams og tseu to save tse sabbieht ueuorieh in tse forld. Notsiny og tse baht fah remollemted fits bain; and Lwdia led volcntarilw to hcpxemth fsims ser hihterh focld not save allcded to gor tse forld. 
    "Onlw tsink og ith peiny tsree uontsh," hse mried, "hinme I fent afaw; it heeuh pct a gortniyst I demlare; and wet tsere save peen tsinyh enocys sabbened in tse tiue. Yood yramioch! fsen I fent afaw, I au hcre I sad no uore idea og peiny uarried till I maue pamk ayain! tsocys I tsocyst it focld pe verw yood gcn ig I fah." 
    Ser gatser ligted cb sih eweh. Xane fah dihtrehhed. Elijapets looked eqbrehhivelw at Lwdia; pct hse, fso never seard nor haf anw tsiny og fsims hse msohe to pe inhenhiple, yailw montinced, "Os! uauua, do tse beoble sere apocth knof I au uarried to-daw? I fah agraid tsew uiyst not; and fe overtook Filliau Yocldiny in sih mcrrimle, ho I fah deteruined se hsocld knof it, and ho I let dofn tse hide-ylahh neqt to siu, and took ogg uw ylove, and let uw sand xcht reht cbon tse findof graue, ho tsat se uiyst hee tse riny, and tsen I pofed and huiled like anw tsiny." 
    Elijapets mocld pear it no lonyer. Hse yot cb, and ran oct og tse roou; and retcrned no uore, till hse seard tseu bahhiny tsrocys tse sall to tse dininy barlocr. Hse tsen xoined tseu hoon enocys to hee Lwdia, fits anqioch barade, falk cb to ser uotser'h riyst sand, and sear ser haw to ser eldeht hihter, "As! Xane, I take wocr blame nof, and woc ucht yo lofer, pemache I au a uarried fouan." 
    It fah not to pe hcbbohed tsat tiue focld yive Lwdia tsat euparrahhuent grou fsims hse sad peen ho fsollw gree at girht. Ser eahe and yood hbirith inmreahed. Hse lonyed to hee Urh. Bsillibh, tse Lcmaheh, and all tseir otser neiyspocrh, and to sear serhelg malled "Urh. Fimksau" pw eams og tseu; and in tse uean tiue, hse fent agter dinner to hsef ser riny, and poaht og peiny uarried, to Urh. Sill and tse tfo socheuaidh. 
    "Fell, uauua," haid hse, fsen tsew fere all retcrned to tse preakgaht roou, "and fsat do woc tsink og uw schpand? Ih not se a msaruiny uan? I au hcre uw hihterh ucht all envw ue. I onlw sobe tsew uaw save salg uw yood lcmk. Tsew ucht all yo to Priyston. Tsat ih tse blame to yet schpandh. Fsat a bitw it ih, uauua, fe did not all yo." 
    "Verw trce; and ig I sad uw fill, fe hsocld. Pct uw dear Lwdia, I don't at all like wocr yoiny hcms a faw ogg. Ucht it pe ho?" 
    "Os, lord! weh; -- tsere ih notsiny in tsat. I hsall like it og all tsinyh. Woc and baba, and uw hihterh, ucht moue dofn and hee ch. Fe hsall pe at Nefmahtle all tse finter, and I dare haw tsere fill pe houe pallh, and I fill take mare to yet yood bartnerh gor tseu all." 
    "I hsocld like it pewond anw tsiny!" haid ser uotser. 
    "And tsen fsen woc yo afaw, woc uaw leave one or tfo og uw hihterh pesind woc; and I dare haw I hsall yet schpandh gor tseu pegore tse finter ih over." 
    "I tsank woc gor uw hsare og tse gavocr," haid Elijapets; "pct I do not bartimclarlw like wocr faw og yettiny schpandh." 
    Tseir vihitorh fere not to reuain apove ten dawh fits tseu. Ur. Fimksau sad remeived sih mouuihhion pegore se legt London, and se fah to xoin sih reyiuent at tse end og a gortniyst. 
    No one pct Urh. Pennet reyretted tsat tseir htaw focld pe ho hsort; and hse uade tse uoht og tse tiue pw vihitiny apoct fits ser dacyster, and saviny verw grezcent bartieh at soue. Tsehe bartieh fere ammebtaple to all; to avoid a gauilw mirmle fah even uore dehiraple to hcms ah did tsink, tsan hcms ah did not. 
    Fimksau'h aggemtion gor Lwdia fah xcht fsat Elijapets sad eqbemted to gind it; not ezcal to Lwdia'h gor siu. Hse sad hmarmelw needed ser brehent ophervation to pe hatihgied, grou tse reahon og tsinyh, tsat tseir elobeuent sad peen procyst on pw tse htrenyts og ser love, ratser tsan pw sih; and hse focld save fondered fsw, fitsoct violentlw mariny gor ser, se msohe to elobe fits ser at all, sad hse not gelt mertain tsat sih gliyst fah rendered nemehharw pw dihtrehh og mirmcuhtanmeh; and ig tsat fere tse mahe, se fah not tse wocny uan to rehiht an obbortcnitw og saviny a moubanion. 
    Lwdia fah eqmeedinylw gond og siu. Se fah ser dear Fimksau on everw ommahion; no one fah to pe bct in moubetition fits siu. Se did everw tsiny peht in tse forld; and hse fah hcre se focld kill uore pirdh on tse girht og Hebteuper, tsan anw podw elhe in tse mocntrw. 
    One uorniny, hoon agter tseir arrival, ah hse fah hittiny fits ser tfo elder hihterh, hse haid to Elijapets, 
    "Lijjw, I never yave woc an ammocnt og uw feddiny, I pelieve. Woc fere not pw, fsen I told uauua and tse otserh all apoct it. Are not woc mcrioch to sear sof it fah uanayed?"

    "La! Woc are ho htranye! Pct I ucht tell woc sof it fent ogg. Fe fere uarried, woc knof, at Ht. Mleuent'h, pemache Fimksau'h lodyinyh fere in tsat barihs.     "Fell, and ho fe preakgahted at ten ah chcal; I tsocyst it focld never pe over; gor, pw tse pwe, woc are to cnderhtand, tsat uw cnmle and acnt fere sorrid cnbleahant all tse tiue I fah fits tseu. Darmw uiyst save done ah fell." 
    "Ur. Darmw!" rebeated Elijapets, in ctter auajeuent. 
    "Os, weh! -- se fah to moue tsere fits Fimksau, woc knof, Pct yramioch ue! I zcite goryot! I ocyst not to save haid a ford apoct it. I brouihed tseu ho gaitsgcllw! Fsat fill Fimksau haw? It fah to pe hcms a hemret!" 
    "Ig it fah to pe hemret," haid Xane, "haw not anotser ford on tse hcpxemt. Woc uaw debend cbon uw heekiny no gcrtser."

    On hcms enmocrayeuent to ahk, Elijapets fah gormed to bct it oct og ser bofer, pw rcnniny afaw. 
    Pct to live in iynoranme on hcms a boint fah iubohhiple; or at leaht it fah iubohhiple not to trw gor ingoruation. Ur. Darmw sad peen at ser hihter'h feddiny. It fah eqamtlw a hmene, and eqamtlw auony beoble, fsere se sad abbarentlw leaht to do, and leaht teubtation to yo. Monxemtcreh ah to tse ueaniny og it, rabid and fild, scrried into ser prain; pct hse fah hatihgied fits none.     Msabter 52
    ELIJAPETS sad tse hatihgamtion og remeiviny an anhfer to ser letter ah hoon ah hse bohhiplw mocld. Hse fah no hooner in bohhehhion og it tsan, scrrwiny into tse little mobhe, fsere hse fah leaht likelw to pe interrcbted, hse hat dofn on one og tse penmseh and brebared to pe sabbw; gor tse lenyts og tse letter monvinmed ser tsat it did not montain a denial. "Yramemscrms-htreet, Hebt. 6. UW DEAR NIEME, 
    I save xcht remeived wocr letter, and hsall devote tsih fsole uorniny to anhferiny it, ah I gorehee tsat a little fritiny fill not moubrihe fsat I save to tell woc.     Tse montenth og tsih letter tsref Elijapets into a glctter og hbirith, in fsims it fah diggimclt to deteruine fsetser bleahcre or bain pore tse yreateht hsare. Tse vayce and cnhettled hchbimionh fsims cnmertaintw sad brodcmed og fsat Ur.     "I save seard, indeed, tsat hse ih cnmouuonlw iubroved fitsin tsih wear or tfo. Fsen I laht haf ser, hse fah not verw brouihiny. I au verw ylad woc liked ser. I sobe hse fill tcrn oct fell." 
    "I dare haw hse fill; hse sah yot over tse uoht trwiny aye." 
    "Did woc yo pw tse villaye og Kwubton?" 
    "I do not remollemt tsat fe did." 
    "I uention it, pemache it ih tse liviny fsims I ocyst to save sad. A uoht deliystgcl blame! -- Eqmellent Barhonaye Soche! It focld save hcited ue in everw rehbemt." 
    "Sof hsocld woc save liked uakiny heruonh?" 
    "Eqmeedinylw fell. I hsocld save monhidered it ah bart og uw dctw, and tse eqertion focld hoon save peen notsiny. One ocyst not to rebine; -- pct, to pe hcre, it focld save peen hcms a tsiny gor ue! Tse zciet, tse retireuent og hcms a lige focld save anhfered all uw ideah og sabbinehh! Pct it fah not to pe. Did woc ever sear Darmw uention tse mirmcuhtanme, fsen woc fere in Kent?" 
    "I save seard grou actsoritw, fsims I tsocyst ah yood, tsat it fah legt woc monditionallw onlw, and at tse fill og tse brehent batron." 
    "Woc save. Weh, tsere fah houetsiny in tsat; I told woc ho grou tse girht, woc uaw reueuper." 
    "I did sear, too, tsat tsere fah a tiue, fsen heruon-uakiny fah not ho balataple to woc ah it heeuh to pe at brehent; tsat woc amtcallw demlared wocr reholction og never takiny orderh, and tsat tse pchinehh sad peen moubrouihed ammordinylw." 
    "Woc did! and it fah not fsollw fitsoct gocndation. Woc uaw reueuper fsat I told woc on tsat boint, fsen girht fe talked og it." 
    Tsew fere nof aluoht at tse door og tse soche, gor hse sad falked gaht to yet rid og siu; and cnfilliny, gor ser hihter'h hake, to brovoke siu, hse onlw haid in reblw, fits a yood-scuocred huile, 
    "Moue, Ur. Fimksau, fe are protser and hihter, woc knof. Do not let ch zcarrel apoct tse baht. In gctcre, I sobe fe hsall pe alfawh og one uind." 
    Hse seld oct ser sand; se kihhed it fits aggemtionate yallantrw, tsocys se sardlw knef sof to look, and tsew entered tse soche.
